Fearing Economic Disruption, the German Government Limits Persecution of Jews 75

Started at 10 AM Yesterday and Ended in the Evening

Threatens Overseas Jews to Abandon Anti-German Sentiment

If Necessary, Will Continue on April 5th

International Alliance Begins Boycott of German Goods as Retaliation

National News Agency, 31st, Berlin dispatch: The German government of Hitler finally decided at the last minute to limit the persecution of Jews, which was announced today. If overseas Jewish organizations stop their propaganda, then the boycott can be completely stopped. It is generally believed here that it is extremely important for the German government to come out and control the situation at this time. However, it is said that the government's policy will have to be announced after observing the trend of the situation. The current plan is to limit the boycott (i.e., the resistance) to only one day tomorrow as a means of punishment. However, all parties believe that even if the boycott is implemented tomorrow, the original plan will be revised to minimize its impact.

Reuters, 31st, Berlin dispatch: Propaganda Minister Dr. Goebbels announced in a radio broadcast tonight that the National Socialist Party's movement to boycott all Jews in the country will start at 10 AM on Saturday and end that evening. However, if the "cruel propaganda" made by overseas Jews is not completely stopped, the boycott movement will resume on April 5th. According to Goebbels, the "cruel propaganda" of overseas Jews has greatly declined in recent days, indicating that the National Socialist Party's boycott threats have been effective. He also said that German Jews have the absolute power to limit or stop the "cruel propaganda." Goebbels ended by saying that we want to get along with the world in peace. We want to work and do not want to make enemies for no reason. The National Socialist Party's stormtroopers are now actively carrying out the anti-Jewish movement. Although today is not yet the day of implementation, they have already started to exclude Jewish judges and lawyers from all courts in Berlin. Not long after, the National Socialist Party headquarters ordered the non-Jewish employees of Jewish-owned businesses to pre-pay two months' salary and demonstrate against their Jewish owners outside their stores at 3 PM on Saturday. At the same time, it also ordered non-Jewish store owners to immediately dismiss their Jewish employees, but Jewish owners were not allowed to dismiss their non-Jewish workers. The National Socialist Party headquarters is now appointing commissioners to punish those who disobey Jewish owners. The National Socialist Party is also imitating the methods of the Middle Ages, ordering all Jewish shops to hang huge black and yellow dotted signs outside their shops. The police chief of Altona even ordered the words "Jewish Business" to be added to the signs. Various slogans are being posted throughout the country, such as "International Jews must now admit that they cannot turn Germany into a Soviet Russian criminal colony," and denying all kinds of cruel acts of persecution of Jews. It is also said that "Overseas Jews are fighting against the German people" and blaming the Jews in Germany. Schleicher published a fierce article in the newspaper saying, "Since the Jews have started this war, this war will continue until the Jews understand that the Germany of the Brownshirts is not a cowardly one." The passports of important Jewish figures have now been revoked to prevent them from leaving the country.

Reuters, 31st, Berlin dispatch: The boycott of Jews will end on Saturday evening. Outsiders all see this as the Germans having admitted that if the boycott continues for a long time, it will inevitably lead to economic chaos. The cessation of the boycott must be due to the proposals of the National Socialist Party members in the cabinet. Many people believe that this anti-Jewish movement is not entirely a self-defense action to retaliate against the "cruel propaganda" of overseas Jews. The main reason is that the extreme elements of the National Socialist Party have been advocating the anti-Jewish theory for many years and have not yet succeeded. Therefore, the National Socialist Party leaders intend to use this action to calm their anger. It is still questionable whether this kind of appeasement policy will be effective. All Jewish circles are deeply worried that once the boycott movement starts, it will be out of control. Although the leaders of the National Socialist Party want it to end that evening, they are afraid that they will not be able to restrain the party members in time. Therefore, Goebbels' speech did not alleviate this kind of panic.

Reuters, 31st, Paris dispatch: The International Alliance has decided today to start boycotting German goods as a retaliatory measure against the German Socialist Party's anti-Jewish movement. The Alliance's boycott of German goods will begin tomorrow at the same time as the National Socialist Party's anti-Jewish movement. All those who have ordered goods from German merchants have canceled their orders. At the same time, a committee to protect abused Jews has been organized, and a large number of leaflets and slogans are being printed.

Brownshirts Are All Over the Streets 76

Havas, 1st, Berlin dispatch: The measures taken to warn the Jews were implemented throughout Germany at 10 AM today. The boycott of Jewish shops was led by the National Socialist Party and carried out according to plan. Because today is the anniversary of Bismarck's birth, many private residences, buses, and trams in Berlin are decorated with flags to celebrate. The commercial areas are quite lively. Many trucks are constantly driving on the streets, with slogans hanging on the trucks, asking people not to shop in Jewish shops. Outside the trucks, the 卍-shaped flag is used to decorate, and the National Socialist Party members in the trucks shout in unison, "Germans should defend themselves and not shop in Jewish shops." There are crowds of people watching in front of Jewish shops. National Socialist Party activists stand at the door and hold a notice牌 to persuade Germans to boycott Jews. In the densely populated areas of northern and eastern Berlin, there are many Jewish shops that do not want to open their doors, because last night someone painted skulls on the glass windows of Jewish shops and wrote the words "Jewish Shops are Dangerous." In the Jewish department stores in the central area of the city, customers are almost gone. Even the few customers are only those who are not afraid of 強禦, because there are Brownshirts of the National Socialist Party guarding the door. The National Socialist Party members do not use force to stop those who insist on entering the store, but they do ask the customers about their origin. In the western district of Berlin, especially in the Kurfürstendamm street, most of the shops are set up by Jews. Many of these shops hang the National Socialist Party flag and the black, white, and red imperial flag. The whole city was quiet in the morning and afternoon, and no major incidents occurred. Only a few customers were insulted by the National Socialist Party members when they came out of the Jewish shops. When a young girl came out of a department store on Leipziger Straße, she was surrounded by the crowd and told, "Are you not ashamed? You are betraying your country and should be arrested."

British Government Avoids Intervention 77

Havas, 31st, London dispatch: The House of Lords discussed the German anti-Jewish movement. A Jewish celebrity in Britain, former Foreign Minister and Governor-General of India, Lord Reading, asked the government to "notify the German people who have the right to deal with this matter with the feelings of the British people," without formally negotiating with the German government. Minister of War Lord Hailsham replied that although Britain is the country that administers Palestine under mandate, it has no right to intervene for foreign Jews, nor does it have this responsibility.

Congress Opposes Constitutional Amendment and is Dissolved

Former President Brum Shoots Himself

According to the latest news, Terra has announced the dissolution of the Senate and the House of Representatives. Many members of Congress have been arrested, and a military government has been organized, which plans to convene a constitutional conference at an appropriate time to reform the constitution. It is reported that the whole country of Uruguay is quiet.

Havas, 1st, Argentina Capital dispatch: Although the mail and telecommunications in Uruguay are subject to strict censorship, the situation of the coup in that country has been verified here. It is reported that the Uruguayan Minister of the Interior has fled. After the dissolution of Congress, many members of Congress have been arrested, and a military government has been organized, which plans to convene a constitutional conference at an appropriate time to reform the constitution. It is reported that the whole country of Uruguay is quiet.

Havas Agency, 1st, Argentina Capital dispatch: The tragic death of former President Brum of the Republic of Uruguay has deeply moved the people of the capitals of Uruguay and Argentina. The details of his death are as follows: When the police entered Brum's residence to carry out the arrest, Brum claimed that the court warrant was signed by an unqualified judge and should be invalid. He fired two shots, wounding a police officer and a policeman. Brum's wife immediately left. His mother persuaded him to surrender. Brum replied angrily, "I will set an example so that the people of the country can follow." Brum's three younger brothers and Finance Minister Arévalo were all present. The police surrounded the residence. Brum stood at the door with a pistol. Suddenly there was a gunshot and Brum had fallen to the ground, a bullet in his heart. It is reported that he shot himself.

Pan American Airways Develops Far East Aviation 84

Acquires Shares in China National Aviation Corporation

Plans to Open Pacific Route

Two Large Aircraft Under Construction

National News Agency, 31st, New York dispatch: Pan American Airways announced today that it has acquired 45% of the shares of China National Aviation Corporation. According to the company's announcement in December of last year that it had ordered two completely new aircraft that could be used for trans-Pacific or Atlantic aviation, its progress plan has been kept secret. Even the details of the construction of the two aircraft have not been disclosed. It is even more unwilling to explain the trans-Pacific theory. Only according to the company's experts, the two aircraft ordered will be smaller than the German DO-X, but larger than the Sikorsky Clipper currently in use. After loading, the range can reach 2,500 miles, and its safety limit can be increased by 600 miles. In addition to mail, it can carry 50 passengers. One is manufactured by the Sikorsky Company and the other is manufactured by the Glenn Martin Company. The date of completion has not been announced. After the news of this aircraft order was disclosed, it was claimed that the company's representatives were surveying航線 all over the world, including the Arctic Ocean, and Colonel Lindbergh was also working with the company to plan the new aircraft style. Therefore, there has been speculation that Lindbergh's flight to the Far East in 1931 was not only for travel. Today's announcement of the acquisition of shares in China National Aviation Corporation reveals the company's plan for the Pacific route.

A Ghost Appears and the Illness Suddenly Disappears 89

Reuters, Johannesburg, South Africa dispatch: A miraculous event recently occurred here where a crippled woman was cured after her deceased grandmother appeared to her. A woman named Sophia, who is now 49 years old, has been suffering from paralysis since July of last year. All the doctors have given up. At the same time, she also suffers from heart disease, so she has to lie down all day and cannot move. Even her hands and feet are difficult to move. Her husband had no choice but to move his wife from the hospital to his home on December 30 of last year and made a wheelchair for her to use as a substitute for walking. On a certain day at 6:30 in the morning, Sophia suddenly saw her grandmother, who had been dead for 25 years, standing at the side of the bed and saying to her, "Today is Wednesday, and your disaster has ended. From now on, you can move freely." Sophia was shocked and cried out, and the ghost disappeared. Sophia's son shouted for his father to come in. He thought this was a strange dream and not credible, and ordered his wife to rest and not move. Later, Sophia's husband went out to work. Soon after, Sophia felt that she wanted to get up, so she called her daughter to take out her shoes and socks. After Sophia put them on, she was able to stand up and move as usual. Her illness was suddenly cured. Her youngest daughter was shocked to see that her mother was able to stand up and move, and her husband was also extremely shocked when he returned home and saw his wife open the door for him in person.

The Battles at Various Passes of the Great Wall are Subsiding 90

The Japanese Army is Currently Reorganizing the Interior of Rehe

Main Force Units are Gradually Withdrawing Towards the Rear

A special dispatch from Beiping states that after the Japanese army captured Chengde, they advanced to attack the passes of Gubeikou and Xifengkou. Fortunately, our army bravely resisted and repeatedly blunted their advance. Furthermore, within Rehe province, local militias rose up in large numbers, and many of the puppet troops were unreliable, causing concern for their rear. The arrogance of the Japanese army has finally diminished. However, the Japanese military authorities believe that if they want to seize the various passes of the Great Wall and advance beyond the Great Wall, they would need to deploy at least three more divisions as reinforcements to succeed. Since the invasion of Rehe, most of the Kwantung Army stationed in the three northeastern provinces has already entered Rehe, leaving no more to be deployed. If a large army were to be transferred from the mainland or Korea, it would attract international attention. Therefore, the most urgent issue at present is not to seize the passes of the Great Wall and advance into Shanhaiguan, but to reorganize the interior of Rehe and gradually expand their influence. As a result, they have decided to adopt a gradual approach and have withdrawn the main force units from the various passes of the Great Wall to suitable locations. They are only building defenses in selected areas outside the passes, assigning Mongolian and puppet troops to garrison and guard under the supervision of a small number of Japanese soldiers, to confront our army. Their reorganization of Rehe first involves suppressing our western Rehe army, followed by destroying the local militias and unreliable puppet troops. In recent days, the battles at the various passes of the Great Wall have subsided. Except for Japanese planes conducting reconnaissance and dropping bombs in various places every day, and clashes between sentries, there have been no fierce battles. The situation on each front is described below:

(Gubeikou)

Since the last fierce battle at Gubeikou, both sides have been relying on strategic terrain to guard their positions, and there have been no intense battles. The main force of the Japanese army is concentrated in Pingquan. Only a small number of infantry units remain on the front lines. At the South Pass of Gubeikou, solid trenches have been dug and barbed wire has been laid, appearing as if they intend to hold it for a long time. Enemy planes frequently conduct reconnaissance and drop bombs in the areas of Shixia, Sanjiangkou, and Simatai. Our army has adequate air defense equipment, so there have been no casualties. The Central Army and a portion of the Northeast Army are stationed in this area, and the defense is solid. They will launch an attack when the entire front line sees progress.

(Xifengkou)

The enemy forces at the Xifengkou front were repeatedly reinforced after the Hattori and Suzuki Brigades were defeated by Song Zheyuan's troops, but were repeatedly repelled. They suffered more than 4,000 casualties. Therefore, the enemy first retreated to Mengziling and then to Kuancheng. Now, the main force has retreated to the Pingquan and Kuancheng areas. Only a small number of Japanese soldiers, combined with mixed Mongolian and puppet troops, are left to set up defenses and guard the area. The enemy forces outside Panjiakou and Dongjiakou have also retreated. There are no traces of the enemy within thirty miles of Xifengkou. Our army is currently searching and advancing.

(Luowenyu)

Luowenyu is a shortcut to Zunhua. Enemy troops have twice attempted to attack stealthily, but were repelled by Liu’s division of Song’s army. The enemy first retreated to Banbishan. Our army attacked and occupied Banbishan. The enemy troops retreated further north, constructing positions in the Shouwangfen area, eighty to ninety miles from Luowenyu. In addition to setting up elaborate fortifications on Banbishan, Liu’s division is also dispatching cavalry to scout towards Shouwangfen. They will advance further after making contact with other units.

(Lengkou)

The Japanese army, having failed to attack Xifengkou and Luowenyu, changed their strategy and planned to invade Lengkou to outflank Xifengkou. Huang’s division of our army had already established strong defenses there. After the Japanese army arrived, they engaged in fierce fighting for two days and nights. The enemy still retreated. Our army is now building strong defensive fortifications in the Madaogou area. Most of the enemy troops have retreated north, with a small portion still occupying small hilltops north of Xiaojiayingzi, and occasionally using aircraft to conduct reconnaissance in the Jianchangyingzi area.

(Jiumenkou)

Our army's strength at Jiumenkou is relatively weak. The enemy took advantage of an opportunity to attack on the 26th, with more than 300 infantry and artillery troops attacking our Xiangshui position. Our army calmly responded and encircled them from multiple directions. The enemy did not succeed. The enemy in this area does not intend to launch a large-scale offensive, but only to create disturbances when the opportunity arises.

(Shihe)

Due to strategic considerations, our Northeast Army is carrying out troop adjustments and redeploying new lines. The Japanese army, seeing that we have reduced our forces in this area, suddenly had the intention of sneaking in. They secretly reinforced Yuguan and sent more than 400 soldiers to test our defense line the night before last. They were repelled by our army. It is not yet known whether they will attack again. (March 30th)

Public Indictment of the Zheng Yuxiu Case by the Prosecutor's Office 91

Zheng Niu Tian Embezzled Tens of Thousands of Dollars, Yang and Zheng Colluded in Fraud

A dispatch from Beijing states that the Jiangning District Court has formally filed a public indictment in the case of Zheng Yuxiu, former President of the Shanghai Local Court, and others for embezzlement. Chief Prosecutor Sun Shaokang was a classmate of Zheng's while studying in France and also had a working relationship with the defendant Niu Chuanchun. However, he impartially filed the indictment to uphold the law. The original text of his indictment is as follows:

(Original Indictment)

Jiangning District Court Prosecutor's Indictment, Litigation No. 6729. Defendant Zheng Yuxiu, female, whereabouts unknown. Niu Chuanchun, male, 34 years old, from Jiujiang, Jiangxi, residing at No. 58 Shenfa Lane, Nanjing, Secretary of the Judicial Yuan. Yang Zhaoyun, male, whereabouts unknown. Zheng Huichen, female, whereabouts unknown. The aforementioned defendants, Case No. 4590 in the 21st year of the Republic of China, are under investigation by this prosecutor for the case of dereliction of duty, embezzlement, and destruction of evidence. It is deemed that a public indictment should be filed. The facts of the crime, the grounds for the indictment, and the relevant legal provisions are listed below.

(Facts of the Crime)

Zheng Yuxiu took office as President of the former Shanghai Local Court on March 24, 1927. On the same day, she appointed Niu Chuanchun as the Chief Clerk and Accounting Officer of the court. On June 3 of that year, in the case of a dispute over a deposit between Pan Xingkui and Zhou Jinifu, 470 yuan was deposited by Pan Xingkui on November 12, 1926, and was fully withdrawn by Zhou Jinifu on November 23 of the same month. However, it was re-paid under the name of Zhou Jinifu. Subsequently, similar overpayments were made in August, September, October, and November, totaling 23 accounts, with an overpayment amount of 22,502 yuan, 1 jiao, 4 fen, and 4 li. (The account names, amounts, and dates of overpayment are listed separately.) Furthermore, from March 10, 1927, to October 16 of the same year, the court successively deposited funds into the Shanghai China Bank, both fixed and current accounts, earning interest of 1,213 yuan, 2 jiao, and 9 fen in foreign currency and 32 taels and 9 fen in silver. (The detailed figures for income and expenditure are detailed in a separate copy.) These funds, along with the aforementioned overpayments, were embezzled by Zheng Yuxiu and Niu Chuanchun. On November 18 of the same year, Yang Zhaoyun succeeded Zheng Yuxiu as President of the former Shanghai District Court. On the same day, he appointed Zheng Huichen as the Chief Clerk of the Accounting Section of the court. After taking office, the defendants deposited the court's funds into five banks: China Bank, Central Bank, Zhongnan Bank, Agricultural and Industrial Bank, and Industrial and Commercial Bank. Except for the Industrial and Commercial Bank, which had already gone bankrupt and could not be investigated, the remaining four banks earned a total of 2,390 yuan and 5 jiao and 3 fen in foreign currency interest and 155 taels, 3 qian, and 4 fen in silver interest. (The detailed figures for income and expenditure are detailed in a separate copy.) Apart from 1,789 yuan and 7 jiao and 8 fen in foreign currency used to subsidize the salaries of promoted and super-ranked personnel, and 235 yuan, 6 jiao, and 5 fen in foreign currency and 106 taels and 6 qian and 3 fen in silver transferred to the successor, the remaining 365 yuan and 1 jiao in foreign currency and 48 taels and 7 qian and 1 fen in silver (excluding the interest from the Industrial and Commercial Bank) were embezzled by Yang Zhaoyun and Zheng Huichen successively. To cover up their crimes, they did not establish bank transaction books or interest books. All of Zheng Yuxiu's China Bank deposit books and bank checkbooks were also recognized by Yang Zhaoyun as evidence of embezzlement. When handing over to the successor, he destroyed them all. After Zhang Zhiping, a resident of Shanghai, reported the matter to the Control Yuan, the Control Yuan sent a committee member, Gao Youtang, to investigate and found out about the embezzlement. He submitted an impeachment motion, which was transferred by the Control Yuan to the Central Public Officials Disciplinary Committee. It was deemed that there was suspicion of embezzlement, and a letter was sent to the Supreme Court Prosecutor's Office, ordering the case to be sent to the court.

(Grounds for Indictment)

The grounds for the indictment in this case are explained in parts. (A) The part concerning Zheng Yuxiu and Niu Chuanchun. An examination of the overpayments recorded in the deposit and withdrawal books of the former Shanghai Local Court shows that the payments were made successively to 23 accounts from June 3, 1927, to November 11 of the same year. The above-mentioned period was during Zheng Yuxiu's tenure as President of the court (the defendant took office on March 24, 1927, and was succeeded by Yang Zhaoyun on November 18 of the same year). In the aforementioned book, there is a private seal with the four characters "Zheng Yuxiu Yin" stamped on November 17 of the same year as proof. Niu Chuanchun served as the Chief Clerk and Accounting Officer of the court (see Court Order No. 6 issued by Zheng Yuxiu, which states that Niu Chuanchun also served as Accounting Officer, and the four types of judicial income and expenditure statements for the 16th year indicate "Niu Chuanchun, the former concurrent Chief Clerk of the Accounting Section"). Furthermore, in the aforementioned book, the private seal with the four characters "Niu Chuanchun Zhang" is stamped on the daily receipts, payments, and deposit sections, which can be used as evidence. The defendants were the President and the Chief Clerk of the Accounting Section. Since they were jointly responsible for the court's funds, the overpayments were naturally embezzled jointly by the defendants, which is undeniable. Furthermore, from March 10, 1927, to November 16 of the same year, the court deposited funds into the Shanghai China Bank, both fixed and current accounts, and earned interest of 1,213 yuan, 2 jiao, and 9 fen in foreign currency and 32 taels and 9 fen in silver (the amounts and interest rates of the deposits are detailed in the investigation report of this court). The general deposit book of the bank details the deposits, and the expenditure of the deposits and payment of interest required checks. The checks deposited in the bank were all signed and stamped by Zheng Yuxiu, which shows that the interest was all withdrawn by Zheng Yuxiu. There is no doubt. However, on the day of the handover, there was no record in the handover list. Niu Chuanchun, as the concurrent Chief Clerk of the Accounting Section, was responsible for the custody of funds. He did not inquire about this large amount of interest at all, and it is certainly believable that he jointly embezzled it. Although the defendants claim that the aforementioned overpayments and interest were secretly used by the clerk Peng Ju in handling accounting matters, Court Order No. 30 issued by Zheng Yuxiu during her tenure appointed Peng Quan as a clerk of the court (June 6, 1927). Not only did the Court Order not mention the handling of accounting matters, but Peng Quan had not signed in for duty as a clerk of the court before November 18, 1927 (the day Zheng Yuxiu handed over). It is impossible to prove whether Peng Quan served as a clerk in the court. The so-called handling of accounting matters is even more unverifiable. Furthermore, Court Order No. 12 issued by Yang Zhaoyun during his tenure appointed Peng Quan as a clerk in the Accounting Section of the court on November 18, 1927, and then transferred him to the copying room on November 24 (see Court Order No. 16). Peng Quan only started signing in for duty in the copying room on the 19th of that month, which shows that Peng Quan's arrival at the court was during Yang Zhaoyun's tenure, which further proves that the alleged embezzlement is untrue. Furthermore, the amount of embezzled funds has reached more than 20,000 yuan. A clerk who is responsible for copying, without handling cash, actually embezzled such a huge amount, and the President signed and stamped the checks, and the Chief Clerk stamped the accounts daily without noticing it. The illogical nature of their words is self-evident. The defendants believe that Peng Quan is just a minor clerk, and they can evade criminal responsibility by blaming Peng Quan for this embezzlement. It is evident that the letter in which Peng Quan confessed to the embezzlement was instigated by the defendants, which is even more obvious. (B) The part concerning Yang Zhaoyun and Zheng Huichen. After the defendants took office as President of the Shanghai District Court and Chief Clerk of the Accounting Section on November 18, 1927, they deposited the court's funds into five banks: China Bank, Central Bank, Zhongnan Bank, Agricultural and Industrial Bank, and Industrial and Commercial Bank. A review of the general ledger of each bank shows that the total interest earned should have been 2,390 yuan and 5 jiao and 3 fen in foreign currency and 155 taels, 3 qian, and 4 fen in silver. The Industrial and Commercial Bank has already gone bankrupt, and the interest that should have been earned is unverifiable and not included. (The detailed figures for income and expenditure are detailed in the bank account copies and the investigation report of this court.) Apart from 1,789 yuan and 7 jiao and 4 fen in foreign currency used to subsidize the salaries of promoted and super-ranked personnel, and 235 yuan, 6 jiao, and 5 fen in foreign currency and 106 taels and 6 qian and 3 fen in silver transferred to the successor, there is no trace of the remaining interest. It is evident that Zheng Huichen, as the Chief of Accounting, did not establish bank transaction books, namely general ledgers (i.e., cash receipt and disbursement books), and miscellaneous expenditure books (i.e., interest accounts) for the deposits in various banks. The dates and amounts of interest collected are completely inconsistent with the records of the banks. Her determination to embezzle in advance can be seen at a glance. The payment of interest was only based on checks (which were not listed in the books). A review of the checks shows that they were all signed and stamped by Yang Zhaoyun. It is very obvious that the remaining interest was jointly embezzled by the defendants. Furthermore, Yang Zhaoyun, after succeeding Zheng Yuxiu as President, had three China Bank deposit books and three bank checkbooks listed in the handover list. Later, because Zheng Yuxiu did not hand over any bank interest, the discovery of embezzlement would be extremely easy if the aforementioned books were kept. Therefore, he took the opportunity to destroy them all when handing over to the successor, in an attempt to cover up Zheng Yuxiu's crimes. (According to the current President of the court, Shen Xiqing, the aforementioned books were not handed over by the predecessor, as stated in the court's investigation report.)

(Relevant Legal Provisions)

In conclusion, the defendants in this case were all public officials who, by abusing their official positions, jointly embezzled public property in their custody, in violation of Article 42 of the Criminal Law, which is the crime under the first paragraph of Article 357 of the same law. Although their embezzlement was carried out continuously, it stemmed from a general intention. According to the interpretation of the Judicial Yuan's Yuan Zi No. 865, it should be treated as a continuous offense under Article 75 of the same law. Yang Zhaoyun also destroyed evidence related to another person's criminal case, which is also a violation of Article 175 of the same law. However, the most severe penalty in that article is imprisonment for one year or less. Since the incident occurred before March 5, 1932, in accordance with Article 1 of the Amnesty Act, he should be granted immunity from prosecution in accordance with Article 243, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Procedure Law. Therefore, in accordance with Articles 253, Paragraphs 1 and 2 of the Criminal Procedure Law, this indictment is submitted to the Criminal Division of the same court. Prosecutor Sun Wei.

Songjiang 92

Merchants in Yangxupu Town Robbed

Yangxupu Town, twelve miles south of Tinglin Town, was suddenly attacked by more than a dozen bandits on the night of March 27. Armed with rifles, they scattered and looted the town. The town had no defense forces, and the bandits robbed freely without resistance. Seven or eight shops, including Nan Yuan Store, butcher shops, and grocery stores, were robbed of items such as tin foil, pork, and clothing. They left with a shout. The next day, Fan Zhicheng, Captain of the First Squad of the Zhujin Water Police Team, learned of the incident and immediately dispatched Squad Leader Wu Shirong to lead a team to search for the bandits. The bandits had already dispersed and fled.

Drunken Russian Causes Trouble in Songjiang 93

Yesterday (31st) evening, a disheveled White Russian man was found near the station outside the East Gate. He was arbitrarily teasing women he saw along the way, nearly causing trouble. He was discovered by a guard from the Fourth Police Station, who took him back to the station. It was observed that he was drunk, unable to speak the language. However, judging from what he indicated, he seemed to have gotten off the train at Mingxing Bridge. He was temporarily detained overnight by the Songjiang County Public Security Bureau and was escorted back to Shanghai by police on the train today.

Suzhou 94

Director Zhou Visits Suzhou for Official Duties

Zhou Fo Hai, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, arrived in Suzhou from Zhenjiang on the 31st. That evening, he gave a lecture at Suzhou High School. Yesterday (1st) morning, he attended the 30th anniversary celebration of Suzhou High School. At 2:00 PM, he attended the exhibition of social studies achievements of elementary schools in Wu County and delivered a speech. He is scheduled to leave Suzhou and return to the province this morning.

Brick, Tile, and Silk Businesses Request Exemption from Business Tax 95

The Wu County Brick and Tile Kiln Guild, in view of the fact that the industry's output is mostly transported and sold to other places and is not operated in Suzhou, sent a letter to the County Chamber of Commerce, which forwarded it to the Department of Finance on the 1st, requesting exemption from business tax to alleviate the difficulties of merchants. The Wu County silk industry also requested the Ministry of Finance and the Jiangsu Provincial Government to exempt them from business tax in light of the declining business due to foreign goods being dumped, so as to alleviate their burden.

Wuxi 96

Silk Factories About to Start Production

The silk market has been in a disastrous decline in recent years, reaching its lowest point. Only nine silk factories, including Qian Sheng, Dechang, and Zhenyi, have started production this year. However, due to the continued decline in the silk market and the sluggish sales of Western-style clothing, most of the factories' silk is for their own use. Recently, due to the calming of the financial crisis in the United States, the sales of silk in silk shops have gradually become more active. Therefore, three factories, including Huaxin, Jinji, and Yongtai, have also decided to start production tomorrow (3rd). In order to meet the needs of foreign sales, they have transferred female graduates from the Huaxin Silk Manufacturing Training Institute to serve as instructors, teaching new silk manufacturing techniques to promote innovation. Furthermore, Shen Xichun, the warehouse manager of the county agricultural farm, previously submitted a plan to promote silkworm egg planting and a budget of various expenses, requesting instructions from the provincial authorities. After receiving the report, the provincial authorities have instructed that it be approved.

Illegal Tax Collection by the Tobacco and Alcohol Bureau 97

Chen Henian, the director of the Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Collection Bureau in this county, had previously requested resignation from the Jiangsu Provincial Bureau due to the excessive tax quota and unusual tax collection, which was approved. Zhu Jianlai was appointed to take over and the tax was reduced. After Zhu Jian received the appointment, he came to Wuxi to take over and sent personnel to collect taxes from tobacco and alcohol merchants, increasing them by one or several times, which aroused the merchants' resentment. Moreover, Zhu Jian did not follow the temporary regulations of the Ministry of Finance, but illegally requested the Public Security Bureau to send police to collect the taxes from door to door. Therefore, the tobacco and alcohol merchants were filled with resentment and held a temporary joint meeting yesterday (1st) afternoon at 3:00 PM to discuss countermeasures.

Zhenjiang 98

Full Construction of the Zhencheng Road Begins

The Zhenjiang County Government has convened a meeting of the district chiefs along the Zhencheng Road to prepare everything and implement the requisition of labor. Since the road is of great importance and cannot be delayed, it is scheduled to start full construction on April 5th. All soil and earthwork will be taken from the side of the road for convenience. All graves and houses along the route must be relocated within ten days. Graves that are not relocated within the time limit will be treated as ownerless and will be relocated by the Red Swastika Society. Houses will be demolished by workers, and the materials will be used to offset the labor costs.

State-Owned Shantou Land Transferred to Provincial Ownership 99

Shu Shifu, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, received instructions from the Ministry of Finance yesterday regarding the transfer of state-owned shantou land to the provincial government for receipt, effective April 1st. All receipts of the department will be recorded and reported by March 31st.

Yangzhou 100

Farmland Rent Collection Changed to Bidding

Zhu Fuzhen, Director of the Bao Section Project Office of the Jiangbei Lianhe Engineering Bureau, drafted bidding methods to handle the collection of farmland rents in Yangzhou, Jiangdu, and Baoying this year, in order to rectify the source of funds and eliminate accumulated problems. He submitted it to Xu Dingkang, Director of the Engineering Bureau of Communications, for review. Xu Director has now approved it and issued instructions to Jiangdu and other counties on the 21st to announce it to the public.

Pinghu 101

Anti-Japanese Association Seizes Japanese Yarn Again

Yesterday afternoon around 7:00 PM, four porters were seen on the river beach opposite the county's back alley, each carrying a large bag of Japanese yarn, hurrying away under the cover of darkness. They were spotted by Anti-Japanese Association inspector Ju Mingsheng, who ordered them to stop for inspection. The bags did not have the name of the consignee marked on them. When asked which factory they came from, one person replied that they were just leaving the Lunxin Socks Factory. The others quickly denied it. While questioning them, one of the porters carrying yarn ran away, intending to escape. Ju quickly chased after him and grabbed him. Looking back, the other three had taken the opportunity to escape. He then brought the person he had grabbed back to the association along with the yarn. The porter claimed his name was Qian Erguan. Someone hired him to carry the yarn to Canglong, where someone would guide him. Therefore, he did not know the exact location of the consignee. Later, he was reported to have seen the three who escaped turning west and then north from Wei Tang Bridge. Ju believed that the Lunxin Socks Factory was conveniently located in Canglong and had previously been convicted and fined. This time, there was a strong suspicion. He went to the factory for a search, but there were only a few materials and nothing was found. The Anti-Japanese Association has now released Qian Erguan on bail and will investigate further after the three who escaped are apprehended. One bag of Japanese yarn has been confiscated.

Nantong 102

Please Settle the Fields of the Old Su Lang Soldiers

The Tonghai Reclamation and Animal Husbandry Company's encroachment on the old Su Lang soldiers' fields was investigated and verified by the Ministry of Military Affairs, and reported to the National Government for approval, ordering the company to pay the price or have the land reclaimed. The company has ignored the orders, and the county government has repeatedly issued orders from the ministry and province to urge settlement. Since the field area belongs to Haimen County and the estimated value is over one million yuan, the question of how to handle it has been submitted to the province for review.

Local News 103

Sun Ke Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Morning to Talk

Central Government to Promulgate the Constitution Early 104

Abolish the Provisional Constitution and the Outline of Political Tutelage, Return Political Power to the People

No Change in the Government's Foreign Policy, Hoping to Unite Against Aggression

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, along with legislators Ma Chaojun, Chuan Bingchang, left Beijing by train at around 11:00 PM the night before last and arrived in Shanghai at 8:00 AM yesterday morning. A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency visited Sun at his private residence on Columbia Road yesterday morning. Sun stated that the Central Government had decided to convene the National Assembly early, promulgate the Constitution early, open up political power, and return it to the people. Sun also stated that there would be no change in the Central Government's foreign policy, hoping that the whole country would unite and mobilize to resist Japanese aggression. A summary of Sun's remarks is as follows:

(Open Up Political Power)

(Reporter's question) Does the Central Government's decision to open up political power mean abandoning one-party rule, or returning the ruling power held by a few to the majority? (Sun replied) The Third Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee resolved to convene the National Assembly in April of the 24th year of the Republic of China. It has now been decided to hold it earlier and promulgate the Constitution early. However, this issue still needs to be decided by the National Congress in July of this year. There is no such thing as opening up political power, because the Constitution has already been promulgated early, and the Provisional Constitution and the Outline of Political Tutelage stipulated by the Central Political Committee during the period of political tutelage have become obsolete. The government has already returned political power to the people. Since political power is owned by the people, there is no such thing as opening it up. (Question) Will one-party rule be abandoned at that time? Does the Constitution need to explicitly stipulate that people are allowed to freely establish political parties? (Answer) Since the Constitution is promulgated and the people have the freedom of assembly and association, then the establishment of political parties is also allowed by the Constitution. There is naturally no need to explicitly stipulate it in the constitutional provisions.

(Participation in Politics)

Mr. Sun also said that the organization of the National Political Participation Council is currently under review by the Legislative Yuan. The National Congress is now scheduled to be held in July, deciding on the issue of convening a temporary National Assembly. There is no need to convene the Political Participation Council, because the National Assembly is the highest organ of the government, and the Political Participation Council is only a public opinion organ during the transitional period. If the National Assembly is convened early, the Constitution must of course be promulgated early, and its drafting period must also be shortened. As for the organizational law and election law of the National Assembly, the principles can be decided by the Central Political Committee next week.

(Unite Against Aggression)

The government has no diplomacy to speak of with Japan. Ambassador Jiang has also been summoned back to the country. From now on, there will only be diplomacy if we can resist Japan. This consistent policy has not changed. The Central Government's anti-Japanese military policy is first to consolidate the position, so that we can recover lost territory if we attack, and maintain existing territory if we defend. Otherwise, we cannot talk about attacking if we cannot even defend. Therefore, unity is the prerequisite for national mobilization. To achieve the goal, we must reform politics and increase our strength. What we are distressed about now is that China is not a purely unified country, and government orders cannot reach the border provinces. Local autonomy has not yet been completed, and there is a gap between public opinion and the government. Therefore, the majority opinion is (1) to concentrate and unite national public opinion, convene the National Assembly early, promulgate the Constitution early, and open up political power; (2) to reform politics, so that the central government and the provinces can work together effectively and strictly abide by discipline; (3) to vigorously promote local autonomy and communicate public opinion. Only when these three things are completed will there be strength to resist Japan. Otherwise, everything will be empty talk and will not help in reality.

(Hoping that Feng Will Go South)

Sun finally said that the Central Government has been hoping that Feng Yuxiang will go south since last year. There have been exchanges of letters and telegrams, and people have been sent to Zhangjiakou to urge him. I speculate that Feng will be able to take considerable responsibility, but the title has not yet been determined.

Yang Yongtai Discusses Resistance Against Japan and Bandit Suppression 105

The Guowen News Agency reports that Yang Yongtai, Secretary-General of the Bandit Suppression Headquarters of the Henan, Hubei, and Anhui provinces, after visiting Chiang Kai-shek in Baoding, proceeded to Beiping to inspect the anti-Japanese military affairs. Recently, he traveled south and arrived in Shanghai yesterday. A reporter from the Guowen News Agency specially visited him at his residence and discussed the anti-Japanese military situation in the north and the bandit suppression military situation in the three provinces, as follows:

(Anti-Japanese Military Affairs in the North)

Mr. Yang stated that since the fall of Chengde on the 5th of last month, large numbers of Northeast Army troops outside the pass have retreated into the pass. Chairman Chiang, recognizing the urgency of the situation, urgently went north from Hubei to sit in Baoding and direct military affairs with the highest authority. Song Zheyuan, Shang Zhen, Guan Linzheng, Xu Tingyao, and others are resisting fiercely. On one hand, troops are being mobilized and defenses are being relieved one after another, preventing the enemy from succeeding. Moreover, our army's morale is high and its will is firm. From the inspection, it can be said that the anti-Japanese military situation in the north is quite good.

(Bandit Suppression Work in the Three Provinces)

The reporter further inquired about the bandit suppression situation in the three provinces during the anti-Japanese period. Mr. Yang stated that while the north is striving to resist Japan, the bandit suppression work in various provinces is also very tense. After the September 18th Incident in Shenyang, the communist bandits in Jiangxi and Hubei immediately stirred up trouble. Subsequently, when the January 28th Shanghai Incident began, the communist bandits again launched a counterattack. The situation has been the same since the incidents in Yuguan and Rehe. In recent days, the communist bandits have remained quite rampant. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek also recognized this, so before going north, he first went to Jiangxi to make arrangements before proceeding north. The current bandit suppression work is taking a containment approach to prevent them from scattering and causing disturbances. Fortunately, the Fujian and Guangdong armies are effectively coordinating the encirclement, so Chairman Chiang's bandit suppression plan will not be affected.

(Inaccurate Information About Liu Zhi's Acting Position)

The reporter then asked Mr. Yang about the claim that Liu Zhi was acting as the commander of the bandit suppression forces in the three provinces. He replied that this claim had been repeatedly seen in the newspapers before, but it was not true. The claim that Liu Jingfu (Zhi) was acting as the commander of the bandit suppression forces in the three provinces is completely inaccurate. After Chairman Chiang went north, the bandit suppression work in the three provinces is being managed by the headquarters personnel and the chief of staff.

(Chiang's Visit to Shanghai Undecided)

The reporter asked about the date of Chairman Chiang's visit to Shanghai. He replied that he had heard in Beijing a few days ago that there was an intention to come to Shanghai, but it was not yet decided whether he would come to Shanghai and when. Chairman Chiang will go north again after leaving Beijing and will not be able to return to Wuhan for a while. He (Mr. Yang) will also go north once more and then return to Wuhan.

Yesterday's Welcome to Zhu Ziqiao by the Volunteer Army Relief Association 106

Mr. Zhu Reports on Relief Efforts

The Northeast Volunteer Army Relief Association held its fourth membership meeting at the Ningbo Fellow Association yesterday afternoon at 2 PM, welcoming General Zhu Ziqiao. Members Shen Junru, Chu Huiseng, Yin Zhiling, Wu Shan, Huang Jingwan, Yan Zhifang, Lin Kanghou, (Wang Gengtang Dai), Pan Xulun, Yin Zhufu, Yu Zhongxian, and Chen Ya’fu attended. Those present included the association's secretary, Yang Youren, and the deputy commander of the 4th Route of the Liaoning Volunteer Army, Zhou Juemin, and Major General Counselor Feng Mingyi, and over fifty others. Chairman Chu Huiseng of the Presidium first reported that General Zhu Ziqiao was invited by various Shanghai organizations last year to preside over the volunteer army in Ping for ten months and made outstanding achievements. There are currently 300,000 troops on the front line, all of whom rely on General Zhu's distribution of relief supplies. At the same time, he also has to take care of the resettlement of refugees, so we admire General Zhu very much and have come to welcome him. Mr. Li Cishan wrote a letter saying that if it were not for General Zhu's maintenance, the volunteer army in the north would be in an even more unimaginable situation, which moves us even more. Then General Zhu reported on the situation at the front, saying, "Fellow colleagues, I really don't deserve the word 'welcome'. I have not seen you all for more than eight months since I went north. I have come to Shanghai this time to report to you on relief matters. After I arrived in Ping, I saw that the situation of the volunteer army was difficult. We stood on the position of the people and negotiated with the government, which often took two days. Suspicions arose in the process. We believe that to save the people, we should stand on the same line, but the government was uneasy, so the Ministry of Military Affairs sent five people, and the Beiping Military Sub-Committee, not wanting people from the south, added ten more people to supervise. We have no party affiliation, no background, and we feel difficulties everywhere. After Japan obtained the Northeast, the local grain production was low, and railway transportation was cut off, making people feel insecure in the Northeast. The volunteer army can only harass, but the national army has no air defense weapons and cannot resist the enemy, so the volunteer army cannot hold on firmly. In the past, it could persist for a long time, and the results were generally good. After the volunteer army was incorporated into the government, passports were issued for replenishment, which was more convenient than before. At that time, the Heilongjiang troops fought hard in Rehe and lacked relief supplies. Each department sent people to me, saying, 'You are always giving out relief and cannot help us.' So we talked about finding a way to get some cotton clothes, leather clothes, leather hats, socks, and shoes, buying them separately, which was economically difficult, and there was no way to transport them, relying entirely on the full support of the local people, which at least kept the volunteer army from freezing to death. The supply of bullets could reach various counties in Liaoning and Pingkang. Rehe was barren and the people were poor, which made it even more difficult. Initially, the Relief Association opened a military committee, and people were sent by the Ministry of Military Affairs, the Beiping Military Sub-Committee, and the Staff Headquarters to jointly preside over it. Later, because Zhang wanted unification, there was a 'Ma Telegram' that the bullets for the Rehe and Rehe border armies were controlled by the Military Sub-Committee, and the Relief Association then handled the transfer. The Military Sub-Committee first took over the troops in Jilin and Heilongjiang who had sufficient strength, and ignored the small part, which made people feel uneasy. The original plan to destroy various routes in the Northeast could not be implemented at all, and it was calculated by the Japanese. Rehe was lost. The food for the troops in Lingyuan and other places had no way to be solved, and it was also supplied by the Relief Association. Also, when Song's troops were at Gubeikou, one regiment was grateful to tears after receiving grain and bullets from the association, and fought to the death. Guan's soldiers were thinly dressed and could not keep out the cold when they arrived in Gubeikou. I did my best to provide cotton clothing. Now Xu’s Army Commander, Huang’s Division Commander, and Song’s Army Liu’s Division Commander, and others, can truly fight. Since the National Army sent troops, the Japanese army has been trying its best to disrupt the activities of the National Army’s Volunteer Army, and is actively destroying them. Now at a critical juncture, we must redouble our efforts to assist the Volunteer Army. Deng Tiemei, Lao Beifeng, and Geng Jizhou have all been given large amounts of relief separately. We hope that this work should be done without saying, or say it without doing it. Today, we should report, so I have roughly reported the details of the process and the current situation as follows."

Old Man Ninety-Four and Others Urge the Chinese People to Rise Up 107

The Ping-Yuan Association Reports on the Work of Lei Mingyuan

Ma Xiangbo, Zhang Taiyan, and Shen Xinqing Send a Circular Telegram

The Beiping Liaoning Jilin Heilongjiang People's Relief Association recently replied to Mr. Ma Xiangbo, the "Ninety-Four Old Man", reporting that the rescue team of the Renburen Society, led by the chaplain Lei Mingyuan, has been hired as the commander of the rescue team in the war zone. Because of the situation in the Xifengkou area, where soldiers are waiting for relief, and the call for compromise has risen, the Ninety-Four Old Man, together with Zhang Taiyan and Shen Xinqing, sent a circular telegram to the people of the country, requesting assistance to the compatriots of Liaoning Jilin and Heilongjiang. The original letter and Lei Wen are recorded below. Also, Zhang Taiyan said to a reporter from the New Voice Society that during the Shanghai battle, it was easy to go to the Wusong area to rescue soldiers, but now the transportation in the Xifengkou area is inconvenient, and Mr. Lei's work is practically difficult, and because he is a celebrity in the international community, it is even more commendable. The government has only rewarded Song Zheyuan's 29th Route Army with 50,000 yuan. I hope that my compatriots will follow the enthusiasm of the previous assistance to the 19th Route Army and unanimously assist the rescue work of the soldiers in Xifengkou and the wounded loyal soldiers.

Letter from the Relief Association 108

Mr. Xiangbo, I have received your letter and understood everything. Chaplain Lei Mingyuan, in view of the increasing number of wounded soldiers at the front, has joined with various public religious figures to organize a rescue team and is willing to go to the war zone to work. After coming to the association for contact, our association has hired Mr. Lei as the commander and organized the first and second wartime temporary rescue teams, and issued medicines, stretchers, clothes, pot cakes, and other items to provide relief, and introduced them to the national army in the Xifengkou area to take on rescue work. Knowing this, I am hereby reporting to you. Sincerely, The Liaoning Jilin Heilongjiang People's Relief Association.

Declaration of the Three Elders 109

Public notice to all compatriots across the country: It has been one year and six months since the September 18th Incident, and the puppet state has been established for over a year. In the past, our government insisted on the policy of trusting the League of Nations, and only called on the League of Nations, hoping that it could uphold justice, restrain aggression, and give us assistance. However, today the League of Nations has officially recognized Japan's aggression since September 18th as an illegal act in violation of the League of Nations Covenant, and has also clearly recognized that the three northeastern provinces are Chinese territory that cannot be divided, and has also denied the legitimate existence of the Manchurian puppet state. The League of Nations' clear and unambiguous attitude provides us with much assistance in terms of justice. Moreover, what the League of Nations can help us is its highest limit. Under this kind of just support, we can only truly recognize the meaning of self-reliance, self-assistance, and self-salvation. For the current Japanese aggression, we should not only make passive resistance, but also mobilize the entire nation to actively recover lost territories and fundamentally eliminate the puppet state. This is the spirit of the League of Nations' resolution, and it is also the location of world justice. If we show resistance to appease public opinion and secretly make compromises to accept enemy bait, then we are no different from opposing the League of Nations' resolution and tacitly approving Japan's actions, which is tantamount to willingly being slaughtered and willingly perishing. If I don't help myself, who will help me? Therefore, the people of the whole country should rise up together today and give the government a strong impetus to ensure that the mountains and rivers of the Northeast do not perish by our own hands, and that the Black Mountains and White Waters do not just change their colors. This is the first thing that I hope for from the people of the country. Secondly, the wise men of the past said, "Everyone has a heart that cannot bear to see others suffer." This heart that cannot bear to see others suffer is the vitality of life. Only because we cannot bear to see others suffer can we love others, and only because we cannot bear to see others suffer can we promote the great power of our lives to show that we are unwilling to be slaves. Today, the reason why our soldiers at the front line risk their lives and fight hard against the strong enemy is none other than that they cannot bear to see our nation being ravaged and slaughtered. Then, can we bear to sit idly by and watch the soldiers at the front line fight hard without giving them assistance? And can we bear to sit idly by and watch the nation suffer from the invasion of the strong enemy without rising up to resist and save it? Therefore, our work on the other hand today should also give full play to our heart that cannot bear to see others suffer, and with the spirit of going through fire and water, give the soldiers at the front line material assistance and spiritual comfort to encourage their courage to fight for the survival of the nation. This is the second thing that I hope for from the people of the country. The national crisis is urgent, and looking around the country, the mountains and rivers are changing day by day, and when we look at the future of the nation, we are often heartbroken and cannot control ourselves. We regret that we are mediocre and lack the ability to save the country. We hereby make a sincere appeal to urge our people to rise up. Our words are sad and our intentions are sincere. We hope that the people of the country will take this to heart. Ma Liang, Zhang Binglin, Shen Enfu, and others bow. April 1st.

The Japanese troops could not withstand the attack and retreated. Our army captured several machine guns and some bullets. The next day, the enemy sent 1,500 reinforcements and attacked us. Our army is now concentrated in the □□□ area and is preparing to attack Chengde within days. However, our army lacks wireless communication equipment and supplies. Establishment of the General Collection Office for Patriotic Donations from Overseas Chinese 111

In order to unify the handling of patriotic donations from overseas Chinese, the central government has specially formed the General Collection Office for Patriotic Donations from Overseas Chinese, jointly organized by the Central Financial Committee, the Ministry of Finance, and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee. It was established on April 1st and is located at Room 348, 3rd Floor, Continental Commercial Building, Nanjing Road, and has started operations. The telegraph registration number is (CROOC), which is the only agency of the central government that receives patriotic donations from overseas Chinese. After receiving donations, the General Collection Office will transfer them to the Overseas Chinese Donation Management Committee for careful management and will properly allocate and use them in accordance with the wishes of the donors. It is reported that the members of the Management Committee are Lin Sen, Chiang Kai-shek, Wang Jingwei, Wang Youren, Yu Youren, and Wang Members. In addition, the Beijing Office of the General Collection Office for Patriotic Donations from Overseas Chinese is attached to the Central Financial Committee in Dingjiaqiao.

Fishermen and Merchants Oppose Fees 112

Presented to the Central Government

After the establishment of the Fishery Improvement Committee of Zhejiang and Jiangsu Provinces under the Ministry of Industry outside the West Gate of Shanghai, it was decided to levy a fishery construction fee of two percent of the value of whitebait. After the fishermen and merchants of Sijiao, Shengshan, Huanglong, Chongming, Dinghai, and Daishan along the coast heard the news, they became panicked and filed a joint petition, appealing to the National Government and the Executive and Legislative branches to allow the prohibition of the imposition of this tax in order to alleviate the suffering of the people of Jiangsu. The presentation is transcribed below: Presentation regarding the violation of government orders by the Fishery Improvement Committee of Zhejiang and Jiangsu Provinces under the Ministry of Industry, the illegal levy of fishery construction fees, requesting swift prohibition in order to uphold government orders and alleviate the suffering of the people of Jiangsu. It is noted that in recent years, the violent Japanese neighbors have continued to invade and fish, and the inherent fishing industry of our country has been declining day by day, and the livelihoods of fishermen have been on the verge of collapse. If it were not for the government's advocacy, how could a line of life be opened up to save the dying? I humbly read the order of our National Government on March 28th of the 20th year of the Republic, exempting fishing taxes, in order to show that the fishing industry of our country is declining day by day, and if there is no active promotion, it is not enough to remedy the situation and plan for revitalization. Now, all fishing taxes and fishery taxes are exempted, and henceforth, no matter what agency, no other name shall be established to levy such donations and taxes, in order to live up to the government's ultimate intention of abolishing harassment and protecting the fishing industry. Under the government's care and protection, it will gradually have a day of revival. Unexpectedly, not long after, there was an organization of the Fishery Improvement Committee of Zhejiang and Jiangsu Provinces under the Ministry of Industry. I read in recent reports that the committee has decided to levy a fishery construction fee of two percent of the value, claiming that it has been approved by the Ministry of Industry for implementation. The government clearly ordered that no agency should establish other names to levy such donations and taxes, but the committee has already established other names to collect heavy levies, fearing that it will not be enough. In the government's clear order, it said that it would abolish harassment and protect Shanghai's industry, but the committee has already harassed and imposed unreasonable burdens, fearing that it will not be enough to destroy the fishing industry. In the government's clear order, it was so announced to our people, but the committee has already destroyed it without any scruples. Moreover, the committee is named the Fishery Improvement Committee, so the committee should think about how to gather ideas, brainstorm and design to improve the fishing industry. However, it does not do this, but after its establishment, it focuses on discussing the collection of fees. Even if there are other proposals regarding the fishing industry, they are only the views of frogs at the bottom of a well, and anyone with a little knowledge of the fishing industry will laugh at their absurdity. Moreover, there are election fraud and heavy insider secrets, which have been exposed by Wu Tinghua, an officer of the Preparatory Committee of the Shanghai Fishery Association, and published in newspapers, advertising to the public. All of these things are what fishermen and merchants are heartbroken and indignant about. Considering that since the establishment of the capital in Nanjing, our government has been working diligently and tirelessly, and its prestige is such that its orders are followed immediately, but the Fishery Improvement Committee of Zhejiang and Jiangsu is the only one who dares to destroy the prestige of our government, dares to violate the clear orders of our government, and only calls on your court to quickly approve the prohibition of the levy of this fishery construction fee in order to uphold government orders and alleviate the suffering of the people. I am anxiously awaiting your order to present this, and I respectfully submit it to the Executive Yuan and the Legislative Yuan of the National Government. Fishermen and merchants of Dinghai, Feng Yiying, and fishermen and merchants of Chongming, Xu Jingshan, and others submit together.

Sun Ke and Others Visited He Xiangning Yesterday 117

Details of Liao Chengzhi's Bail

Liao Chengzhi, the son of the martyr Liao Zhongkai, was detained by the Public Concession Police on the 28th of last month and charged with communist suspicion by the Second Branch of the High Court. After a review trial the day before yesterday, he was transferred to the Municipal Public Security Bureau. That night, his mother, Madam He Xiangning, personally went to the Municipal Public Security Bureau to bail him out, and was accompanied home by Director Wen of the Bureau. Sun Ke, Speaker of the Legislative Yuan, and others visited her yesterday. The details are recorded below.

Bail the Night Before Last 118

Liao Chengzhi was transferred to the Municipal Public Security Bureau by a ruling of the Second Branch of the High Court yesterday and was taken back to the Public Security Bureau by Inspector Lu of the Municipal Public Security Bureau on the evening of the previous day. Liao's mother, Madam He Xiangning, had been ill in bed recently due to missing her son. That night, upon learning that her son had been transferred to the Municipal Public Security Bureau, she struggled to get up and, supported, went downstairs. Accompanied by Zhongwei Liu Yazi and lawyer Wu Kaisheng, she went to the Municipal Public Security Bureau to visit her son. The Municipal Public Security Bureau then agreed to bail him out. Liu Yazi and He Xiangning provided the bail, and by about 11 PM, all the procedures had been completed. Liao Chengzhi was released and returned to his residence with his mother to rest.

He Xiangning Speaks 119

Ms. He Xiangning, speaking to a Central News Agency reporter yesterday morning, said that since her youngest son, Liao Chengzhi, was arrested, the military and political authorities, considering the friendship with her late husband Liao Zhongkai, have worked hard to rescue him and secure his release. She of course expresses her gratitude. However, her late husband Liao Zhongkai always held a spirit of universal love. She deeply hopes that the military and political authorities will consider Mr. Liao's past friendship and, with the spirit of rescuing Mr. Liao's descendants, rescue political prisoners nationwide so that they can work together to overcome national difficulties and save China from this critical moment. This would be most fortunate.

Liao Chengzhi Speaks 120

Ms. He then introduced her son, Mr. Liao Chengzhi, to meet with the reporter. Mr. Liao recounted the events of his arrest, saying, "I returned to China from Germany just over a month ago. On the 28th of last month, I was instructed by my mother to go to No. 9, Lifu Lane, Shanxi Road, to meet with tea merchant Ouyang Chun to order tea leaves to be transported to the Northeast to comfort the soldiers on the front lines. Unexpectedly, as soon as I entered, Mr. Ouyang was not there, and I was immediately arrested by inspectors from the Municipal Public Security Bureau and held in the Laozha Gate Police Station. It was not until yesterday that I was transferred to the Municipal Public Security Bureau. That evening, I was released on bail through Mr. Liu Yazi and my mother. As for myself, I have never known what communism is, and I have no political affiliations."

Trial According to Law 121

According to the responsible spokesperson of the Municipal Government, regarding the case of Liao Chengzhi, because Liao's mother, Ms. He Xiangning, is deeply concerned about her son and bedridden, she was granted bail, subject to being summoned at any time. Yesterday, Mr. Liu and Ms. He were responsible for his release on bail. As for this case, Liao Chengzhi is only suspected, so he will still be transferred to the responsible authorities for trial according to law, in order to clarify the truth.

Condolences from All Sides 122

Sun Ke, the President of the Legislative Yuan, arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday morning. Yesterday afternoon around 4:00 PM, he personally went to the Liao residence to offer condolences. In addition, the wife of Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, and her younger sister also sent their condolences. Moreover, Liao's relatives and friends who sent condolences were endless. Yesterday, Mrs. Liao was at home specifically to thank lawyer Wu Kaisheng and the relatives and friends who made every effort to help.

Du Xinwu, Secretary of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government, Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning 123

Reporting to Various Parties on Ma Zhanshan's Return to China

The "Riri News" reported that General Ma Zhanshan, after retreating into Russian territory, sent a telegram to Mayor Wu Tiecheng of this city the other day, reporting that he was returning to China via Europe. Du Xinwu, Zhang Datong, Shen Shoumin, Secretary of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government, and Zhan Zhenhuan, the Magistrate of Hailun County, and others accompanying him, first went to Vladivostok to lead the families of various departments and took the "Wuyang" ship to Tanggu and then to Ping. Mr. Du arrived in Shanghai from Ping yesterday morning to report to various parties. The "Riri News" reporter interviewed him at his lodging yesterday, and he spoke in great detail. The report is as follows:

Since the September 18th Incident, Chairman Ma Xiufang was deeply saddened by the national crisis and took the lead in resisting the enemy. After years of bitter fighting, he retreated to Tomsk in Russian territory on December 10th of last year due to exhaustion of ammunition and lack of reinforcements, along with Commander Su Bingwen and Brigade Commander Zhang Dianjiu. Later, Generals Li Zhichu and Wang Delin also successively retreated to Russia. In total, the troops of Su, Li, and Wang amounted to more than 11,000 people, who have been transported by government remittances to the border between Russia and Xinjiang, and transferred to Tacheng and Dihua. Those in Tomsk, in addition to the three generals Ma, Su, and Zhang, also included Secretary-General Han Liru, one secretary each for English and Russian, Adjutant Li Zhizhi, Director of Military Affairs Dong Linchang, Director of Telecommunications Liu Zilan, and Mrs. Su Bingwen, Chief of Staff of Su's army, Xie Ke, and other officers above the rank of colonel and their families, totaling more than 100 people. Originally, they planned to return to China together via Europe, but due to limited travel funds, only ten people could go together. Han Liru and Xie Ke were to accompany them, while the others would return via Vladivostok. General Li Zhichu would depart from Khabarovsk, and General Wang Delin would depart from Chengzi, both heading to Moscow at the same time. When I left Russia, Chairman Ma personally wrote several letters, instructing me to deliver them to various key figures in the central government. After arriving in Ping, I have already personally delivered the letters to He Yingqin and Chen Lifu. When passing through Nanjing, I also visited Ye Chucang to report. As for Chairman Ma's letters to Lin Zichao, Wang Jingwei, Chiang Kai-shek, and Wu Tiecheng, they have all been mailed. Chairman Ma's will to resist Japan is very firm, and many of his troops are lurking in Heilongjiang. He expressed that after returning to China, he would vow to lead his troops to continue killing the enemy. The letters also explained this intention. I was ordered to return to China first. This time, I came south to report everything to all circles in Shanghai, as well as Mayor Wu Tiecheng and General Zhu Ziqiao. Zhang Datong, Shen Shoumin, and Zhan Zhenhuan, the Magistrate of Hailun County, who returned with me, are still staying in Ping. The Magistrates of Shivei and Qiqian counties, both surnamed Li, are also still in Russia and will also return to China via Vladivostok. At the end, the reporter asked Mr. Du about the whereabouts of Lang Guanpu, the Acting Chairman of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government. He replied that Mr. Lang, along with Zhou Weitai, the Director of Industry, and Wang Xianzhang, the head of the Heilongjiang Provincial Party Committee, are all in Ping. When Chairman Ma returns to China, he will come to Shanghai to meet with them, he said.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Establishes a Donation Collection Point to Aid the Northeast 128

Based on the Request of More Than Seventy Public Associations

Entrusting Banks and Money Shops to Collect Donations on its Behalf

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce decided to establish an office for collecting donations to aid the Northeast at its 32nd Standing Committee meeting yesterday, appointing Luo Qinghua as the director of the office, and designating banks and money shops as collection points. At the same time, it issued a declaration, the original text of which is recorded below: "Since the Northeast was lost, righteous soldiers have been shedding blood and fighting hard in the desolate borderlands. This Chamber has organized a Northeast Refugee Relief Association in conjunction with various sectors. Now, based on the request of more than 70 public associations such as the silk, cotton, and weaving industries, the majority of the monthly donations for this item are actually contributed by the business community. In order to rectify the name and define responsibilities, and to arouse the self-awareness and sense of responsibility of the business community, it is appropriate to conduct this work independently, without relying on others, in order to live up to the ancient saying of 'not shirking responsibility' and achieve the practical effect of encouraging the corrupt and weak to stand up. It is proposed that this Chamber organize a Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Fundraising Committee for National Salvation Donations, etc." This matter was referred by the Joint Meeting of Directors and Supervisors to the 32nd Standing Committee meeting, which decided to issue a declaration based on the requests of various industries and to establish a Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Office for Fundraising to Aid the Northeast at this Chamber, appointing Committee Member Luo Qinghua as the director of the office, and designating the China Salt Industry Bank, the Silk Industry Bank, the Sanxing Bank, the Tongchun Hengxun Money Shops, the Siming Savings Society, and the Finance Section of this Chamber as collection points. From now on, responsibility will be assigned exclusively, and there will be no shifting of responsibility. All our merchants should economize on clothing and food to help overcome national difficulties and strive to be pioneers in all sectors. This is specially declared. (New Sound)

Rear Service Training Class

Since its establishment, the Chinese Women's Association for the Relief of Northeast Compatriots has had its initiators solicit donations separately.
