(Beiping) This morning on the Shimenzhai line, the enemy launched repeated assaults, engaging in hand-to-hand combat with our troops. Subsequently, over 20 enemy aircraft from an aircraft carrier anchored off Qinhuangdao flew in formation, bombing and strafing our positions for two hours, with bombs falling like a continuous string of pearls. Some of our front lines and villages were heavily bombed, and our troops suffered nearly half of their casualties. (Special dispatch on the 2nd)

(Luanzhou) Frontline dispatch: Intense fighting continued all day in the Shimenzhai area. After dusk, the situation has reached a stalemate. Commander Yao Dongfan is actively recovering troops and replenishing ammunition in a certain location due to heavy casualties, preparing for a decisive battle with the enemy. The Shibei line has shifted to a major defense line in response to the situation. The enemy is also reorganizing and reinforcing, and major battles are expected to continue. (Special dispatch on the 2nd)

(Beiping) In this Japanese offensive, the enemy is using troops led by Li Jichun and others to attack us, using Chinese to fight Chinese, attempting to avoid responsibility for Japanese atrocities. Villages on the Shibei front have been occupied by enemy troops. (Dispatch on the 2nd)

(Luanzhou) After the breakthrough at Shuizhaiyu prevented our reinforcements from Jia Ying from achieving their objective, the regiment and battalion entrenched in Yashuiyu, Chenzhuang, and Liangjiashan were surrounded by superior enemy forces by morning. The fighting was fierce and casualties were heavy, especially in Jiang's battalion. However, they still mustered their remaining courage, broke through the encirclement, and slashed wildly with their swords, killing many enemies. The fighting was also intense on the right flank, with the company of the regiment of the cavalry division in the Yashui River and Shuizhaiyu area still engaging in skirmishes with the enemy. Until after 5:00 PM, the intense sounds of gunfire and artillery from Shimenzhai shook the mountains and valleys. The telephone line to Shimenzhai was cut off after 3:00 PM. While our troops were engaged in hand-to-hand combat, three enemy aircraft bombed and destroyed Haiyang Town again at 4:00 PM. One enemy aircraft also flew to Shenhebao, west of Haiyang, for reconnaissance. (Special dispatch on the 1st)

After our troops' unsuccessful counterattack near Linyu yesterday, by about 10:00 AM today, the enemy launched a fierce attack on our Shimenzhai position and the area near the Yashui River with over 3,000 troops of a new type of unit, and 14 aircraft took turns bombing repeatedly. The battalion of our regiment rushed to the rescue but was surrounded by the enemy. At this time, multiple aircraft from the enemy aircraft carrier in the sea also came to bomb, bombing the entire position until it was nearly flattened and destroyed by 2:00 PM. As of the time of dispatch, fighting was still ongoing. According to captured enemy wounded soldiers, the Shimenzhai area is defended by the 2nd Puppet Garrison Army, consisting of three brigades and six regiments, approximately 6,000 men, dressed like the Japanese army and mixed with many Japanese. The Qiuziyu area is defended by the 1st Cavalry Detachment of the Puppet Garrison Army, led by Ding Qiang, and Zhao Lei's brigade, led by Miao Zibin, totaling 4,000 men, and 400-500 Japanese soldiers. (Special dispatch on the 1st)

Nearby villages were reduced to ashes. Martial law has been declared in Qinhuangdao. (Special dispatch on the 2nd)

Inside Story of Japan's Withdrawal from the League of Nations 231

The Seiyukai Hoped to Regain Power

Saito Government Urgently Needed to Maintain Domestic and Foreign Affairs

(Reuters, Tokyo, March 28) The Japanese Diet adjourned on March 25. Throughout the session, the friendly attitude between the government and the Seiyukai was evident. Now, rumors of a cabinet reshuffle are rampant. Some time ago, it was widely rumored that Prime Minister Saito and Seiyukai President Suzuki had reached an understanding: if the Seiyukai supported the passage of the 1933-34 budget, the current national unity cabinet would resign after the Diet adjourned and recommend the formation of a purely Seiyukai cabinet to replace it. The Seiyukai's friendly attitude during the Diet session was partly due to its hope of regaining power. Although this specific understanding is highly questionable, if the current cabinet resigns, the power to select its successor will largely be in the hands of Elder Saionji. It is said that the Seiyukai's recent opposition to Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations and its insistence on sticking to the end were for this reason. It is clear that the Seiyukai is doing everything it can to prepare for its return to power. When Seiyukai Prime Minister Inukai Tsuyoshi was assassinated on May 15 last year, the Seiyukai held an absolute majority in the House of Representatives. After this act of violence, it was necessary to form a strong and powerful national unity government to cope with the serious domestic and foreign situation. The Seiyukai now believes that the crisis has passed and a national unity government is no longer needed, so it believes that there is no reason not to take back power from Saito now. If the Seiyukai's words are to be believed, the national crisis has indeed disappeared, and a change of cabinet would be easy. However, outside observers believe that restoring a party-led government at this time would be extremely dangerous, perhaps even more so than the internal strife that led to the formation of the national unity government a year ago. There were many reasons why the Japanese people united last year, but the two greatest were the pressure from Geneva and the excitement over the Manchurian Incident. Now that Japan has withdrawn from the League of Nations, foreign condemnation is gradually fading away, and the development of Manchuria is largely settled, no longer as lively as before. Therefore, Japan's unity is likely to weaken. Moreover, taxes are surprisingly high, and the people bear unprecedented burdens and sacrifices. Therefore, the general opinion is that Japan still urgently needs a national unity government today. (Dentsu, Shizuoka, 2nd) Prime Minister Saito arrived at Shizuoka Station at 6:00 PM yesterday and entered the Daito Inn. At 9:00 AM this morning, he took a Shizuoka Prefectural Office car to Okitsu to visit Prince Saionji, reporting on the process of withdrawing from the League of Nations, the deliberations of the 64th Diet, and the recent political situation. The meeting lasted until 11:30 AM, exchanging important opinions for about two hours. At 1:40 PM, he left Shizuoka and returned to Tokyo at 4:55 PM.

Diverse Forms of Anti-Jewish Movement in Germany 233

Some Jewish Stores are Closed, Others Operate as Usual

A Picket is Shot and Killed Inside a Store

Hitler's Stormtroopers Execute the Store Owner's Son

Schleicher Announces That Anti-Jewish Actions Are No Longer Necessary

(Reuters, Berlin, 1st) Berlin's boycott of Jewish people has been poorly organized. Many Jewish stores remained open after the nationwide declaration of a boycott, even with anti-Jewish slogans posted on the windows. Business proceeded as usual inside. Most of the most prominent Jewish stores in Berlin have closed, but not all of the large Jewish stores in the suburbs have done so, and the owners have not yet been disturbed. Many large Jewish stores are now closed, leaving a large number of non-Jewish employees idle. Even these non-Jewish employees do not all agree with the boycott. Many people gather in front of the closed Jewish stores, discussing the matter animatedly, while brown-shirted comrades walk back and forth, posting slogans on the windows to indicate that these are Jewish stores. Today is the day of the National Socialist Party's grand demonstration. Swastika flags and imperial flags fly on Berlin's trams and streetcars, and military bands march through the streets, playing military and patriotic songs. The streets of the Kurfürstendamm are extremely crowded, and many businesses are closed, making the crowd even larger. The anti-Jewish movement on the Kurfürstendamm is very strict. Not only are leaflets posted outside Jewish businesses, but Jewish doctors' offices and other businesses are also being boycotted. What is particularly off-putting is that cameras are set up in front of Jewish businesses, and anyone seen leaving a Jewish business is photographed, so no one dares to patronize them. Today is Saturday, the Jewish Sabbath, so many Jewish people are taking the opportunity to close their businesses. There have been no violent incidents in the Kurfürstendamm area. The train to Denmark today is carrying a large number of passengers, all Jewish people leaving the country. Hundreds of people disembarked in Copenhagen, but many others continued to other parts of Denmark.

Einstein's Savings Confiscated 234

(Havas, Berlin, 1st) The famous scientist Professor Albert Einstein has declared his resignation from the directorship of the Kaiser Wilhelm Institute for Physics and the Prussian Academy of Arts. After Einstein's resignation, the Prussian Academy of Arts issued a statement saying, "We have learned from the newspapers that Einstein has been helping France and the United States spread propaganda, saying that Germany has committed atrocities against Jewish people. The Academy is deeply indignant. Einstein intends to renounce his German citizenship first, and then his Prussian citizenship, so the Academy has no regret for his resignation." After Einstein engaged in anti-German propaganda, his bank savings were seized, totaling 30,000 marks in securities and cash. The German government said that these savings were for treasonous purposes.

(Reuters, Berlin, 1st) The only serious incident related to the nationwide anti-Jewish movement in Germany today occurred in Kiel. A picket was shot and killed in front of a furniture store. National Socialist stormtroopers immediately attacked the store, stormed inside, and arrested the store owner's son, who was said to be the shooter. After the man was taken into custody at the police station, National Socialists stormed the station and shot him to death. Jewish people who occasionally laughed at the boycott movement or made dissatisfied remarks on the street were arrested. Pickets are also monitoring many famous restaurants and businesses, which is surprising, as it was not previously known that they were Jewish-owned. Employees of Jewish stores gathered outside the store and joined National Socialists in a demonstration at the square outside the former imperial palace to protest what they called the "atrocity propaganda" launched by foreign Jewish people. National Socialists today went to a bank where the famous scientist Albert Einstein had savings, checked his account, and confiscated all of his securities worth 25,000 marks and 5,000 marks in cash. It is said that Einstein recently arrived in Antwerp, Belgium, from New York and declared that if Germany interfered with the freedom of thought of its people, he would never return to Germany.

(Reuters, Munich, 1st) General Schleicher, leader of the anti-Jewish movement, announced here tonight that, according to telegrams from overseas, there is no need to continue the boycott after April 5, next Wednesday. Therefore, the boycott will be limited to one day and will end nationwide tonight.

The Discovery and Development of the Red Scare Incident in the Japanese Naval Port 252

According to the Tokyo Kokumin Shimbun, the four naval personnel arrested last September for the red scare incident in the Japanese naval port have had their preliminary hearing at the military court concluded. All newspapers have also been released to publish the details simultaneously. This case involves Hengjiro Nishi, a third-class sailor on the warship Haruna, Yoshiji Yoshihara, a third-class sailor on the warship Nagato, and Takeshi Kawada, a third-class sailor on the warship Yamashiro, who were instructed by the Communist Party headquarters to carry out the red scare plan in Yokosuka Naval Port in January of last year. The plan involved using rest time to first instill communist ideas, and then organize red scare classes. By May of the same year, they used the summer vacation time to hold secret meetings at the home of the mastermind, carefully studying communism. In July, they went to Tokyo, where Mao Tanigawa, the Minister of Military Organization of the Communist Party, secretly provided red scare materials and planned the propaganda outline, in order to strengthen and expand it in the navy. In September, a theft suddenly occurred on the warship Haruna. During a strict inspection of the crew, Nishi, feeling guilty, hurriedly discarded all the red scare documents in a dustbin, where they were found. At the same time, evidence of contact between Kawada and Yoshihara was found in Nishi's letters. With this, the case was completely exposed. Since the incident, the naval authorities, in order to prevent the spread of red scare ideas, have conducted detailed investigations into the identities of naval soldiers.

The Fur Trade of Soviet Russia 253

Currently Ranks Second in the World

TASS Moscow News In the old Russian era, Russia's fur trade was completely controlled by foreign merchants. They collected furs through plunder and uneconomical methods, so most animals were killed off, and some even became extinct. After the revolution, the Soviet government began to restore the fur trade, with remarkable results. The Fur Trust uses the complexity of the climate within the Soviet Union to cultivate various animals. Currently, the Fur Trust manages 140 rabbit farms and 30 wildcat farms. Dozens of farms cultivate animals such as white fox, silver fox, blue fox, sable, and silver sable. The number of artificially cultivated muskrat reaches ten thousand. The fur trade of the Soviet Union currently ranks second in the world, second only to the United States. In northern Soviet Union, such as Kamchatka and the Caucasus Mountains, where human traces are scarce, hunting work has gradually developed. In 1932, the Soviet Union had 40 "hunting stations," which have now increased to 80. The Soviet Union's fur industry has also been developing rapidly in recent years. In the old Russian era, the furs supplied to foreign merchants were all raw materials. Currently, half of them have been processed and dyed by Soviet factories, and many foreign merchants send their furs to Soviet factories for processing. In the last ten years, the Soviet Union has exported furs worth 850 million rubles. Furs account for a huge proportion of total exports, sometimes even reaching 12 percent. The current Soviet Union can be called an international fur market. Each year, when fur auctions are held in Leningrad, fur merchants from various countries come to participate.

The Quantity of Munitions Supplied by Britain to Japan 256

London Correspondence (March 1st)

At Geneva, the British representative, in voting on the Lytton Report, expressed support for the report in order to create the impression that Britain does not agree with Japan's actions in the Far East. In reality, the British government is simultaneously the supplier of munitions to Japan. British Foreign Minister Simon plays the role of peaceful arbitrator in Geneva, endorsing the proposal affirming that Japan is the aggressor. In London, the poison gas company in which Simon is a major shareholder is increasing shareholder dividends. In words, it supports peace, but in reality, it supports war. This is the British Foreign Minister.

It is impossible to point out the exact number of munitions shipped from Britain to Japan. The British government's trade statistics only record the figures for specifically licensed exports of military supplies. In 1929, Japan's total munitions imports from Britain accounted for 17.3 percent. In 1930, the percentage accounted for by Britain reached 30.5 percent. Subsequently, this percentage has increased significantly. The ratio of munitions shipped from Britain to Japan compared to munitions shipped to China is four to one. From this, it can also be seen that Britain favors Japan. British government trade statistics indicate that the quantity of machine guns and bullets shipped to Japan was particularly high from August 1931 to September 1932. From September 1931 to September 1932, approximately 10 million rounds of bullets and approximately 660 machine guns were openly shipped to Japan. In addition, there were many other military equipment. In 1932, a total of 13 million rounds of bullets and 800 machine guns were shipped to Japan. However, this is only the first batch of munitions ordered by the Japanese General Staff. The British munitions industry has become even more vigorous with the development of Japan's military in the Far East, processing and manufacturing day and night. In the last four months, the supply of machine guns alone has been sufficient to supply 54 brigades (at the same time, millions of bullets and auxiliary parts, etc., were shipped to Japan).

According to the "Daily Herald," a certain munitions factory has supplied Japan with 36 million rounds of bullets alone. Another munitions factory has supplied Japan with 1,000 machine guns. This was within eight weeks. Vickers-Armstrong, whose pre-war dividend was only 5 percent, now has a dividend that has increased to 25 percent. Recently, it has also obtained a contract to purchase munitions worth 30 million pounds. A large number of cannons were shipped to Japan not long ago, and now it continues to receive contracts to order a large number of 8.5-pound bombs. According to the "Sunday Express," Vickers-Armstrong is manufacturing for Japan 24 hours a day. To manufacture bomb caps, it has added 700 workers. The Newcastle factory shipped 30 tanks to Japan last November. Vickers-Armstrong-Conceal's Dartford factory is entirely manufacturing hand grenades for Japan.

Finally, it is particularly noteworthy that Japan has been buying ships in Britain. In the last three years, Japan has purchased 76 old ships in Britain, totaling 500,000 tons. Most of these transactions were completed in the second half of last year. Two of them were relatively large, with a maximum draft of 45,000 tons. During the Great War, these British ships were used as transport ships, hospital ships, and armed merchant ships. Japan is also buying ships in the Netherlands, Norway, and Belgium.

As mentioned above, the correct number of munitions shipped from Britain to Japan cannot be obtained from British trade statistics. British munitions factories have their own private methods for selling munitions. The "Sunday Express" claims that many of the munitions supplied by Britain to the Japanese government are shipped through Siam. A large portion of the munitions used on the front lines are shipped directly to certain locations without passing through Japanese seaports.

The magnitude of the munitions that British industry supplies to Japan has reached a level that can no longer be kept secret.

Japan's Preparation for Total War Mobilization (Japan News) 257

Recently, the Scientific Pictorial Publishing House held a symposium on national total mobilization. The attendees were all figures from the Ministry of the Army, such as Yoshio Uetsuki, Chief of the Control Section of the Preparation Bureau; Shizudo Yatari, staff member; Seiichi Yamada of the Mobilization Section of the Preparation Bureau; and Hageo Tanihana, Xiong from the News Class. What they discussed was extremely important. Here is a summary translation, which should clarify the recent preparations for war in Japan.

1. The Future War's Character - Total Mobilization

Needless to say, we all know what the future war will become. Everything is evolving, and war has also evolved greatly from ancient times to the present. In the primitive era, the main body of war was roughly centered on one person or one tribe. However, as society gradually evolved, the main body of war also gradually expanded to nations, tribes, cities, or countries. Also, ancient wars were limited to a portion of the nation, especially a few people advocating the use of force to fight, so the end of the war was attributed to the defeat of the central figure, the extinction of a tribe, or the defeat of an armed group of a tribe, city, or country. However, since the Franco-Prussian War in 1870-1873, a state of evolution has been particularly evident. The French army was almost completely destroyed by the German army. Although the field army was defeated, Gambetta later gathered a force of volunteers, said to be 2.5 million strong. This shows that even if the field army is defeated in this era, the nation can still fight if it still has a strong will to continue the war. Later, although the Sino-Japanese War and the Russo-Japanese War also occurred, they cannot be considered thorough wars, and can be said to have ended halfway. Therefore, the so-called national war form was not demonstrated. If Japan had been defeated at that time, it would have certainly gathered volunteers again to continue the national final battle. As for the World War, needless to say, almost all of Europe participated in the state of war. Its evolutionary footprint has history as evidence. In the primitive era, war was a one-on-one state, but because of the evolution of society, war gradually became various forms. The Franco-Prussian War can be said to be a war of the whole nation, and the World War can be said to be a war of national power. If there is another war in the future, I think that this future war has a very close relationship with all the politics, economy, transportation, and transportation of the world, so the occurrence of war is more like a military war between several countries or a complex war between one country against several countries, rather than the state of a military war between one country against one country like the Sino-Japanese War and the Russo-Japanese War. From this point of view, in the future war, both

The number of soldiers used should be increased compared to past battles, so the need for military supplies should also increase. And, as I said earlier, the method of engagement has also greatly changed, and finally became the so-called war of national power. So, when two countries fight, eliminating the enemy country's will to continue the war is also counted in the tactics. Then, if you want to eliminate the enemy country's will to continue the war, what method should you use? There are many methods. To give one or two examples, using propaganda to eliminate the army's or the nation's belief in victory is also a method. Also, the front plane is very developed. A plane can transport a ton of bombs from a distance and drop them on Tokyo, the political center, or Nagoya, the economic and industrial center, or the Kitakyushu area. This is another method, or use aircraft to bomb industrial cities to destroy their resources. This planned destruction of resources is also a method of engagement. Other methods, such as the starvation policy or economic blockade adopted by Germany against Britain, should also be considered important means of engagement. Recently, a certain country (referring to the Soviet Union) has even issued the statement that there will be no front lines in future wars. In reality, when fighting, bullets will be used, so a war without front lines is impossible. However, a certain country's methods of engagement are like this: on the one hand, fighting on the front line, while expanding the battle line from the rear of the front line to the colonies and within the enemy country, using various methods to eliminate its military force or guide its revolution. It is true that a certain country may be able to adopt such methods of engagement. From this point of view, the future war is no longer linear or planar, but three-dimensional, and the geographical area has expanded from the battlefield to the country. Regarding the equipment of the troops, during the World War, Germany used poison gas to attack secretly, causing the British army to be defeated. Conversely, Britain used tanks to attack the German army, endangering German territory. As such, weapons have made great progress from the war, and new weapons will inevitably be produced in response to the times. Moreover, these weapons will require a large number of iron. Recently, the tendency to use large amounts of poison gas materials has also been clearly demonstrated. If we look at the weapons that various countries are striving for, we can understand that they value the enrichment of aircraft, the development of chemical warfare aircraft, and the increase in the power of guns and cannons. Because to compensate for these, the knowledge of optics, electricity, and dense machinery has been used to the greatest extent in the research of weapons, and various automobiles are used to replace horses in mechanized corps. Such observations of the future war situation show that, from any perspective, a large amount of iron and a large amount of military supplies are needed. This is very obvious. During the two years of the Russo-Japanese War, the Japanese army fired 1.05 million shells. In the Battle of Mukden, the Japanese army fired 330,000 shells in two weeks. However, in the Battle of the Marne in World War I, the French army fired one million shells in one week. The shells used by the Japanese army in two years of the Russo-Japanese War were fired clean by the French army in just one week. Also, in the Battle of Sulm, the French army used 20 million shells in two weeks, while the British army used 14 million shells. If we drop so much iron on the enemy's position, just thinking about these shells, where should these industries be manufactured during wartime? This question will inevitably arise immediately. The Japanese army only has arsenals. It is certainly impossible to produce a large quantity of things there, so it is inevitable to use civilian factories. This is just talking about bullets. However, clothing and food also require a huge quantity. Other things such as medical supplies and veterinary supplies also require a considerable quantity. It is ultimately impossible to manufacture these things in government-owned factories. Expanding the capacity at once cannot be done in a short period of time. Therefore, it is essential to use civilian factories. Other issues such as how to obtain raw materials and where to store the finished products, and how to transport them, and other issues will surely arise if you think about it. These problems should be solved in peacetime. It is impossible to prepare for them when the war breaks out, so we must prepare from peacetime. We call this plan for preparation military industry mobilization.

(To be continued)

Investigation of Bandit Situation in Hubei Province 258

Only Thirty Counties in the Entire Province Are Free of Bandits

Hankou Correspondence After the successive recovery of important bandit areas in Hubei Province, there are still scattered bandits in remote and desolate areas. In order to thoroughly understand the bandit situation, the Hubei Provincial Government has recently telegraphed various districts and counties to conduct detailed investigations. Out of the 70 counties in the province, only 30 counties are completely free of bandits. The remaining 40 counties have not yet been cleared. The reports from various counties are recorded as follows:

(Eastern Hubei District) The Eastern Hubei District has a total of 11 counties. Except for Huangmei, Guangji, Luotian, Qishui, and Huanggang, which are free of bandits, the remaining Qichun County has a small band of local bandits led by Lü Zhaoduan lurking in the Triangle Mountain and Niupi Village areas. They have been repeatedly attacked by local militias but have not been eliminated. In Yingshan County, remnant bandits are hiding in the border area and are also being searched by local militias. In Macheng County, there are remnant bandits led by the fake guerrilla commander Nie Weiwen, the fake independent division commander Qiu Jiangpu, Wang Shaoqing, and the fake independent regiment Li Chengxiang, who are disrupting the Zhangjiatianpu area of Guangshan County in southern Henan Province and the Futiange and Haojiapu areas outside the east gate of Songbu in that county. They have recently been blocked and attacked by local militias and stationed troops and have retreated to areas such as Chengmagang, Xianyangyan, and Duanjiapu. In Huang'an County, there are small bands of the fake Hubei-Henan-Anhui Guerrilla Headquarters and the Northeast Road Commander of Hubei Wu Huan, as well as the battle camps of the fake independent regiment, who are disrupting the He area, Qijiaoshan, Triangle Mountain, Laojun Mountain, Huangpodian, and Qiliping areas of the county, sometimes together and sometimes separate, constantly fleeing. After repeated attacks by stationed troops and security militias in various districts, the southwest of the county has gradually been cleared and will be attacked in the northwest. In Lishan County, remnant bandits frequently harass various places such as Xinfuji, Sanlicheng, Qilidun, Wangyangdian, and Yaojiadian. Last month, a small band of remnant bandits from Huang'an County north of Changlinggang, Zhanadian, and Hongmaoyan in Fenshuiling fled from Huang'an and has been dispersed by troops from the 3rd Division and the 4th Security Regiment.

(Southern Hubei District) The district has a total of ten counties. Puqi, Jiayu, and Wuchang are free of bandits. The Boidun Town area of Xianning County was recently harassed once by remnant bandits of the fake 3rd Division and was repelled. Previously, remnant troops from the fake Southern Hubei Guerrilla Brigade fled in Chongyang County near the Badoushan area bordering Puqi. They have now retreated to the border of Hunan. Remnant troops of the fake independent camp and the fake guerrilla team Fang Ruyan in Tongcheng County frequently harass the area and are now fleeing to Huangpao Mountain. In Tongshan County, the 85th Division and the local militias cooperated to defeat the remnant troops of Ye Jinbo and Xu Jinmen of the fake 16th Army and Dai Dechang of the fake independent regiment. The 82nd Division is searching for the red bandits of Zheng Zhong's remnant troops, who are occupying areas such as Maban'ao in Echeng County, breaking up into smaller groups. In Daye County, there are a few remnant bandits such as Xiang Shengping and Fang Buzhou occupying Longjiao Mountain. Taizimiao and Dawangdian in Yangxin County were previously ravaged by the remnant bandits of Kong Hechong and were subsequently repelled. They are currently being defended against and attacked.

(Central Hubei District) The district has a total of twelve counties. Hanyang, Hanchuan, Tianmen, Mianyang, Jianli, Gong'an, and Jiangling are free of bandits. Previously, a small number of bandit supporters from Songzi fled to Shishou County and have now been eliminated. The bandits in Jingshan County are fleeing to areas such as Changtanbu, Luojiaqiao, and Tuanyuping on the border between Jing and Zhong. They are now fleeing to Zhongxiang County. The bandits in Zhongxiang County are a mixture of local bandits and red bandits from Wang Bingnan's troops. They are now occupying Youjiaji. The bandits in Jingmen County are also fleeing to the Huoyan Kwong area with a group of Wang Bingnan's fake independent division and the remnant troops of Huang Guanbo's fake independent regiment. They have been severely attacked by the army and their strength has been eliminated. There are scattered bandits hiding in the Nielu and Liangtan areas of Qianjiang County, but they are not very active. The Western Hubei District has a total of eighteen counties. Zhijiang, Yichang, Yidu, Xuan'en, Xianfeng, Badong, Enshi, and Jianshi are free of bandits. The bandits in Dangyang County were remnant troops of Wang Bingnan in the Huangchengyan and Putonggou areas and have now been defeated by the national army. There is a remnant band of local bandits led by Zhou Ziheng in Songzi County and is currently being attacked and eliminated. Zigui County was once harassed by the bandits of Wang and left without success. There are two groups of red bandits, Huang Laosi, in Yuan'an County. The remnant group had previously fled to Fuhe Temple but retreated to their old nest after being attacked. There are two groups, Sun Xiuzhang and Lu Jiuzhou, in Xingshan County, who have fled to Changyang. There are local bandits led by Gu Zhixiang in Lichuan County, who have fled to the border of Guizhou. There are local bandits led by Wu Lanfen in Laifeng County, who have fled to the border of Hunan. The three counties of Wufeng, Hefeng, and Changyang all have remnant troops of the major bandit He Long. The Director of Security of the entire province, Fan Xiji, is supervising the attack and elimination.

(Northern Hubei District) The district has a total of nineteen counties. Yingcheng, Yunmeng, Yicheng, Anlu, Gucheng, Zhushan, and Zhuxi are free of bandits. There are gangs of local bandits led by Zhang Hengjin and Liu Tiewu in Guanghua County. There is a gang of local bandits led by Wang Cun in Yingshan County. There are two gangs of local bandits, Sun Xiuzhang and Wei Junbo, in Baokang County. There are gangs of red bandits, Wu Yutang and Huang Yuanbai, in Nanzhang County. There is a gang of local bandits led by Zhang Guozheng in Zaoyang County. There are gangs of local bandits, Kang Caiwu and Gu Dasheng, in Sui County. There is a gang of local bandits led by Wang Si in Fang County. There are several gangs of local bandits led by Wang Liu Peizhai in Yun County. There is a small gang of local bandits led by Zhang Mingzhi in Yunxi County. All are awaiting elimination. Xiaogan and Xiangyang counties have not reported. (March 31st)

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Submits a Petition to the Municipal Government to Expand Merchant Education in Pudong 265

Requesting the Allocation of Incense Money from the Imperial Temple of Immeasurable Blessing

Using Superstitious Funds to Establish Schools

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted a petition to the Municipal Government yesterday, stating: "A petition is submitted regarding a request for a factual report. On March 31st, Xia Xinzhai, Director of the Pudong Branch of the association, reported that Pudong has a dense population and closed-off public sentiment. Commercial knowledge is infantile, and there are many illiterate laborers. The reason for this is that education has not been popularized. The only municipal junior high school in Pudong is limited by funding and is crude and simple. The school building has not yet been constructed, let alone expanded. On the west bank of the river, schools are densely packed, but the costs are high and beyond the means of small commercial classes in Pudong, resulting in an increasing number of young people out of school and more illiterate people. To popularize local education, it is necessary to allocate public funds to supplement the municipal treasury, which is insufficient. According to investigation, the annual incense money income of the Imperial Temple of Immeasurable Blessing in Pudong is approximately more than three thousand yuan. The temple management committee has been established for over two years, and the accumulated funds are considerable. However, how the funds are used is unknown. It is believed that this superstitious incense money is part of the local public fund income. If it can be allocated to local education, the public funds will not be wasted, and the local community will benefit greatly. Moreover, the development of education and the revitalization of commerce have a close relationship with each other. In this era of increasingly advanced global commercial warfare, if we look back at our country, it remains old-fashioned and closed off. There is an urgent need to increase the knowledge of merchants and popularize merchant education so that we can compete and survive. Otherwise, there is no way to save the situation. This is the humble opinion of the petitioner, and we dare to present a brief outline. We propose that your association forward a petition to the Municipal Government to approve the allocation of all annual incense money income from the Imperial Temple of Immeasurable Blessing to local education so that the commercial future will be greatly benefited." The association has investigated that the annual incense money income of the Imperial Temple of Immeasurable Blessing in Pudong is quite large. Although there is a management committee to manage the funds, the funds have not been used for the past two years and are stored in a useless place, which is a pity. The Pudong Branch proposes to withdraw the funds to develop merchant education, turning the useless into the useful and benefiting the local community, which is of great significance. It is reasonable to submit a petition for a factual report and request that your government review and order the relevant authorities to transfer the incense money to Pudong local education for public convenience.

American Warship Collides with French Gunboat 266

Yesterday afternoon at approximately 2:00 PM, the flagship of the American Asiatic Fleet, the USS Houston, was entering the Huangpu River and preparing to drop anchor at Buoys 13 and 14 when a small French gunboat, the France-Chine, was passing by on its way to the Yangtze River. The current was very strong, and there was a strong south wind. As the American warship was moving, the French gunboat was pushed by the wind and collided with it, causing several cracks below the waterline in the middle of the ship. A portion of the deck and several lifeboats were also damaged. The ship immediately sent out a distress signal to Shanghai, and the tugboat Saint Dominic arrived to assist in pumping water to prevent it from sinking. Shortly after, the tugboats Victoria and Alexander also arrived and towed the gunboat to the Qiu Xin Shipyard.

Eleven Umbrella Factories, Including Huali, Xin Dalu, and Others, Suspended Operations Yesterday 268

Small Businesses Formed a Forced Common Sales Market

Four Hundred Unemployed Workers Demand a Thorough Investigation by the Party and Government

Recently, small businesses in the city's umbrella industry have formed a common sales market, forcing the large companies, including Huali, Xin Dalu, Minhua, Senfeng, Litailai, Ruilin, Zhixin, Nanchang, Dongnan, Sanyuan, Dayouyu, and others, to participate, disrupting industry regulations. As a result, they all suspended operations yesterday morning, causing disputes. The details are as follows:

The Truth of the Dispute: According to Liu Quanru of Huali, there are more than 40 umbrella businesses, large and small, in the city. Recently, small businesses, including Huanqiu Yichang, Minhua Erchang, Minhua Song Erchang, Yingfeng Huamei Yichang, Huamei Erchang, Xin Zhen, Huazhen, Taidalun, Lixin, and others, formed a common sales market, forcing all factories to participate. The method is to send the goods to them, and they will issue checks. However, the checks are useless because they have no credit. The market deducts six cents per dozen as a commission for the fund. However, because the profit on umbrellas is low, only two yuan per dozen, it is practically impossible to do so. Moreover, according to the market rules, a fine of 200 yuan will be imposed for private sales of one dozen. Therefore, they had to suspend operations to save expenses.

The Union's Statement: According to Chuan Bichen, a member of the standing committee of the Umbrella Industry Union, the workers' wages in each factory are based on the quantity of goods shipped. They can only maintain their family life by working every day. Now, the factories are ignoring the livelihood of the workers and have suspended operations one after another, causing panic among more than 400 male and female workers. In order to protect the workers, the union petitioned the Municipal Party Department yesterday and scheduled to petition the Social Affairs Bureau tomorrow morning, requesting them to send personnel to investigate thoroughly and mediate as soon as possible to maintain the labor movement.

Accumulated Bandits Attempt to Escape Using a Human Pyramid 270

Sentenced Severely After Being Captured

The accumulated bandit Zeng Fanji (nicknamed Da Jizi, previously mistaken for Xiao Jizi) has the skill of pretending to be sick. Every time he is captured, he uses his skill to escape the law. This time, Zeng and his accomplices, Zeng Chongshan, Zeng Zhixiang, Zhang A'er, Gu Shugen, Zhang Xiao Lizizi, and others, were captured by Chief Detective Lu Liankui, Detective Liu Shaokui, and others, and more than ten cases of armed robbery were found. The bandit again used the old trick of pretending to be sick. After being exposed, he and another thief, Wang Xingzi, were imprisoned in a cell to isolate them from their accomplices. Later, Da Jizi saw an opportunity to take advantage of the darkness and conspired with Wang to escape. They destroyed the windows of the prison and used a human pyramid, placing their feet on Wang's shoulders to escape through the window. However, the next day, he was still captured by Chief Detective Lu and others and sent to the First Special District Local Court for interrogation. At the end of the trial, the sentencing was scheduled for Saturday morning. The detectives in charge sent the bandits and the firearms, one pistol, and four bullets, to the First Special District Police Station. Lawyer Ru Bao Yi also appeared in court. Then, Judge Feng Shide took the seat and asked Zeng and others for their names and ages. He then announced the judgment. Zeng Fanji was sentenced to twelve years in prison for robbery and three years for escaping, to be served concurrently for a total of fourteen years. Zhang A'yi was sentenced to eleven years, Gu Shugen was sentenced to eight years, Zhang Xiao Jizi was sentenced to seven years, Zeng Chongshan and Zeng Zhixiang were each sentenced to two years and six months, and Wang Xingzi was sentenced to one year for helping to escape. The guns and bullets were confiscated.

Handed Over to the Japanese Consulate for Interrogation After Being Arrested

The sports program includes drills, horse racing, and other interesting competitions. It is also reported that the area where sailors and marines of the local warships were previously allowed to go ashore was limited to the Hongkou area. From today onwards, the scope will be expanded. On rest days (Saturdays and Sundays), they are allowed to roam freely on the Huangpu Bund Road, the French Concession Avenue, Nanjing Road, Di Si Wei Road, Bao Xing Road, the Cantonese Cemetery, Jiang Wan Road, the Racecourse, Qing Yun Road, Yang Jia Bin Road, and other places.

Meat Ticket and Kidnappers Captured in Changzhou, Sent to Shanghai 274

The Detective Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, together with the Chinese and Western detectives of the Putuo Road Police Station, captured a large number of kidnappers from Kunshan, Qingpu, and other places who were hiding in Shanghai at No. 291, Binlang Road, on the morning of the 31st. After being interrogated by the First Special District Court, the City Public Security Bureau was allowed to transfer them after providing evidence. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. However, after the fact, the Detective Team continued to investigate and learned that the meat tickets were hidden on a coffin boat near Ben Niu, Changzhou. On the same day (31st), Team Leader Lu Ying ordered Squad Leader Liu Shaoqing, Liu Changrui, and detectives Miao Jinhai, Yang Zhongjin, Ren Shouzhi, Pan Huanzhang, Yin Zhengtian, and others to take a special express train at 3:15 PM to Changzhou. They met with Inspector Xu Shengtong and many police officers from the Changzhou Public Security Bureau. At 2:00 AM yesterday morning, they arrived at Xia Tang, which is one mile away from Ben Niu, and intercepted two bandit boats. The boat license numbers were 25532 and 25543. On the spot, they rescued the meat tickets Zhang Heqing (35 years old, from Hanjiasha, Fengjing) and the woman Qi Wangshi (67 years old, from Sanhe Village, Fengjing) on the first boat.

They seized one rifle with the words "Anti-Smuggling Bureau No. 928" printed on the handle. On the second boat, they arrested the kidnappers Wang Yuchang (21 years old), Yang Yushan (35 years old), and Zhang Shaoxiang (37 years old). They were immediately taken to the Changzhou Public Security Bureau for questioning. The detectives transferred them to Shanghai, and their confessions have been separately interrogated. The First Special District Court will interrogate the bandits captured on Binlang Road and transfer them to be handled together in the same case.

Below is a column about the female employee, and a column about her leisure time.

Amateur Talk

Women's Liberation and Men's Liberation 275

— Zhi

The Chinese women's liberation movement has been around for at least twenty years now. The result of this movement is that a portion of women have gained considerable status in politics and society, which is indeed a welcome development!

So, are they truly liberated? No! Not completely! Even men have not yet achieved liberation, let alone women! All their liberation amounts to is cutting their hair, unbinding their feet, and adding a few rice bowls to their slender hands, or producing a few female committee members or county magistrates on the political stage. Other than that, there is simply nothing!

Since the forces of capitalist imperialism quickly stormed into the gates of the East, and the waves of the global economic panic crossed the East Sea and submerged the East Asian continent, China, the semi-colonial land whose blood and sweat have been completely squeezed dry, is filled with countless wounds and sores in its limbs and organs; the decline of the cities and the bankruptcy of the countryside all present a picture of ruin and decay. Under such circumstances, those "semi-liberated" Chinese women are running into walls everywhere. Indeed, they have been liberated, greatly liberated. Look, many of them are already able to be economically independent. However, the majority of them, like the majority of men, either have jobs but still cannot make a living, or are constantly threatened by the terror of unemployment; some are driven by life to live an inhuman existence of selling their souls, bodies, and labor. They have entered the same fate as men, wearing the same shackles. They, like men, have not been liberated! They have no bread or freedom, only suffering, oppression, hunger, and death!

One shackle has only been partially removed, but another shackle has been put on!

Some women who stand on the superstructure of society, in the special class, even turn around to oppress their toiling sisters and brothers. They have destroyed their own shackles, but they have locked others with even coarser and heavier shackles.

In short, the women's liberation movement of the present era is no longer an antagonistic movement between the two sexes, but rather an antagonistic movement between oppressed men and women uniting against capitalist imperialists and other oppressors. Therefore, the true women's liberation movement should start with the "national liberation movement," and should start with the "whole social movement." It must be understood that the women's problem is only one link in the whole social problem; only when the whole social problem is solved can the women's problem be thoroughly and satisfactorily solved. In other words, true women's liberation is men's liberation, which is also the liberation of "human beings"!

Mass Life

The Rationalized Literacy Shop 276

— Ms. Yiling

Trainee in a Middle School

My sister and I used to be trainees at the XX Girls' School on Zhabei XX Road. We originally wanted to be kindergarten teachers at this school and read a bit on our own. As for the title of trainee, we initially found it a bit strange. Schools are not trading firms or stores, so how could there be trainees? Later, the person who introduced us said that most of the kindergarten teachers at this school were promoted from trainees. Anyone who came for the first time had to learn how to manage children in the kindergarten, and only after three months or half a year would they be promoted to teacher.

But after a week of being there, our wishes vanished. We discovered that the exploitation methods here were even more severe than the rationalized system of factories. On the second day of entering the school, the short, bespectacled female principal transferred us to the general affairs office. She said: "I'm sorry, there are too many people in the kindergarten. Please study in the general affairs office for the time being! As soon as there is a vacancy, we will insert you."

We didn't have anything to learn in the general affairs office, just doing record-keeping work all day long. Whenever a student came to get a book or a calligraphy exercise book, we would record it. This work started at eight in the morning and didn't stop until seven in the evening. Before eight in the morning, we had to go to the kitchen to distribute the side dishes to the boarding students. Each student was only allowed one spoonful of fried soybeans or peanuts and a small piece of fermented bean curd (red fermented bean curd costing seven copper coins per piece had to be cut into eight pieces!). In the evening, we also had to manage the students in the dormitory. On Sundays or holidays, we and some of the elementary school teachers were not allowed to go home. We were only allowed to go home twice a month, but we had to return to school before nine in the evening.

Our principal, Ms. Chen XX, is a translator and has translated several English detective novels. She is also a patriot. She cried over her brother, who was studying in Japan, for marrying a Japanese woman, and she angrily scolded him in front of hundreds of elementary school students. And especially an economist, in addition to hiring one or two junior high school teachers with salaries below thirty yuan, the rest of the kindergarten and elementary school teachers were poor widows with salaries of less than twenty yuan and women who were determined not to marry and had no ability to continue their education. Her annual income totaled tens of thousands of yuan, but she still said that there were not enough funds and often went outside to solicit donations.

As for our trainees' salaries, it was only two yuan per month! My sister and I sat in the general affairs office all day long, unable to leave for even a moment. If the principal saw us sitting there doing nothing, she would tell you to copy lecture notes or sew school uniforms. In short, she would find something for you to do. One night, we were reading a book, and she immediately saw it and brought a can of white paint to tell us to paint the glass windows of the bathroom. Miss Li, who went with us, was so angry that she cried, feeling sorry for herself, but I was so angry that I threw the brush into the toilet.

The kindergarten trainees suffered just as much as we did. In name, they could take one hour of child psychology lessons every week, but they didn't have time to review. Because if the principal saw anyone reading, she would say: "This won't do. If you only read your own cruel society

books, no one will do the school's work!"

Under such circumstances, my sister saw that this was not the way to go and left in the first week! But I endured until winter before leaving.

The Life of a Goddess Who Doesn't Sell Herself 277

— Ms. Jia Yu

Waitress at an Amusement Park

It wasn't even two o'clock yet, and my mother was habitually saying, "Qiaozhen, why aren't you going to the company yet? If you don't go in a little while, you'll have to listen to the boss's nagging..." "I know... You're forcing me to go every day!" I also seemed to have gotten into the habit of answering my mother with a venomous remark every day, and I ran out of the alley and got on the bus.

Page 23

Rogue Young Master 278

— Ms. Pan

(Female Staff Member of a University Registrar's Office)

I am a female staff member of the registrar's office at a certain university. Some people must think that since I work in an educational institution, I interact with people who have received more than ten years of education, and my life must be very satisfactory. Even if I am dissatisfied with my salary and treatment, I shouldn't be in danger of being insulted. However, that is not the case.

Those wealthy university students who specialize in selling their souls, in addition to finding customers in dance halls and female dormitories, also pay attention to me. I am in charge of recording the attendance of university students. Because the school deducts one credit for ten unexcused absences, those who sell their souls often pester me. Sometimes they say that I record too many absences, which causes their credits to be deducted, and they scold me for no reason. In fact, this is not my fault, because it is my job.

Sometimes, they deliberately stand in front of my desk and stare at me. When I ask them what they are doing, they don't answer, but just talk nonsense, beat around the bush, and comment endlessly! These rogue young masters are obviously bored of playing with dance girls recently, and the female students don't pay attention to them, so they do this! Rogue young masters! Let me tell you honestly! I came out to work because I am poor. If I were willing to be a plaything for bourgeois men, would I stay here?

Sometimes, some students from other provinces speak to me in dialects. When I ask them back in English, they don't answer, but just look at me and laugh. It wasn't until later that some female students who understood their language told me that they were asking if I liked them, that I understood. From then on, whenever I heard them ask that question, I would answer in Mandarin like this: "I like you very much! To die for!" They knew that I understood, so they didn't say it anymore!

But I really can't think of a good way to deal with the nonsense of those who sell their souls!

Kept dragging on until the company.

Five o'clock struck, and everyone hurried to change shifts for dinner, to prepare to entertain guests who would eat dinner and go to the game field for tea; otherwise, a swarm of foreign devils would come, and you would be so dizzy from drinking that it would be difficult to cope even if you had eight hands.

The incident started on a Saturday night. On this day, the Beijing opera theater had a new production of "Wen Wu Xiang Qiu", and the audience was particularly crowded. More than a thousand seats were filled with guests, and there were many people standing like standees on both sides of the aisles, and the uniformed supervisors were desperately trying to drive them away. The so-called foreign devils occupied several tables. My table, which usually had few patrons, suddenly had everyone flocking to it as if they had discovered something new. The phrase "difficult to cope even with eight hands" flashed across my mind again, and this situation made me a little anxious.

"Hey! Brew a few cups of tea." A young man, with a rat-like glint in his eyes, said while constantly glancing at my face.

"How many cups, strong, weak?" I asked impatiently.

"Whatever." A man wearing a melon-skin cap and with his sleeves rolled up high replied.

"If it weren't for eating this mixed-up rice, who would be willing to mess around with this bunch of smelly men?" I thought, as I went to get the tea.

"Is six cups enough?" I said, putting the tea in the middle of the table.

"Ah! Not bad! You can hold so many cups in one hand, and still have a towel..." The rat eyes stared even harder, as if he would be happy only if he could swallow me in one gulp.

"What, are they all weak? I want a strong one..." The man with the melon-skin cap quickly interjected.

"I want chrysanthemum tea... Hey! Xiao Wang, ask her to make it. What's the point of drinking hot tea!" The big guy, who hadn't spoken for a long time, now also started to make fun. I retorted, "You said 'whatever,' and I'm not the worm in your stomach. How would I know who likes to drink what?" My eyes were burning with anger, but I still couldn't say anything more venomous to scold them. But I felt that my attitude was enough to make them suffer.

Unemployed Designated Cafeteria 279

Rules

Pick any dish you want,

I won't open if you can't eat it.

Exchange sweat and labor for food,

Sorry, no service when full!

The Zha Ying Trading Company at 378 Beijing Road is looking to hire several salespersons. Regardless of gender, anyone with extensive experience in various businesses may apply.

A certain industrial cooperative has newly invented a type of "Bean Fresh Sweat". Anyone familiar with the soy sauce industry and with sales skills, regardless of gender, may apply. Those interested please come to 233 Qipu Road after 4 PM daily to discuss.

Modern Parents Monthly is planning to hire several special translators and commentators (no gender restriction) to assist in editing affairs. Those who wish to take on this position, please specify their academic qualifications and send one or two of their recent translations for reference and consideration. Please send submissions to the editor of Modern Parents Monthly, Chinese Children's Welfare Association, 20 Museum Road, this city.

A certain organization needs to add a copyist, male, monthly salary of twenty yuan, with room and board provided. Anyone under the age of twenty to forty, with good writing skills, quick writing, and neat calligraphy, who is willing to apply, please send a letter to the Huang residence, 20 Ruifeng Lane, Dongjiaxing Road.

Mr. Yu Huizhong of St. John's University, Van Wang Du, is now looking to hire a tutor, two hours of lessons every evening (5 PM to 7 PM), location at the intersection of Back Road and Cade Road. Regardless of gender, anyone can apply, but must have a high school diploma to be qualified.

Mr. Yang Shangwen of 320 Kengneng Hai Road is looking to hire a tutor. Anyone who is good at chemistry and has insights into the study of various oils may apply.

A certain bi-monthly magazine still needs to solicit submissions, with each article being 2,000 words. Articles about humorous commentary, urban sketches, marriage problems, etc., are welcome. Payment ranges from two to ten yuan per thousand words. If a return postage fee is included, unsuitable articles will also be returned. Please send contributions to Chen Fuhua, 3rd floor, Shanghai Electric Power Company.

A certain import and export company is now seeking someone to solicit customs declaration business, regardless of gender, and anyone may apply. However, no room and board is provided, nor is a salary given, but the commission is generous. Those interested please send a letter to Shen Yifei, 8 Tongyi Lane, Beile Road.

"Yo! What you say sounds very sharp, I didn't see that in you!"

"Okay, okay, don't say much, brew a few more cups!" The eyes of the old green rat relaxed.

"What tea?... How many cups?..." I still asked with the same humble but unyielding tone.

"Strong."

"I want chrysanthemum tea."

I took the towel and gathered everything up and left, but my ears were still listening to them: "Hey! Xiao Wang, you're not wronged to treat us tonight, are you?... This 'widow' is much more beautiful than when she first came, look, she's wearing new clothes tonight..."

Ah! No wonder they are doing me a favor tonight and taking care of my business: it turns out it's because of my new clothes. I carried two cups of tea in my hand, thinking as I walked.

"Why did you only brew two cups of tea, and not bring any hot water? I drank all my cups a long time ago." The little melon-skin cap wanted to try something new again.

When I went to brew tea just now, I saw several full cups there, how did they disappear in a blink of an eye? I knew they were trying to make me unable to leave this place, but I was selling tea, so I couldn't stop them from drinking, right? "Take your time, I don't have four hands!" I was always unhappy with their actions.

"Hey! Why are you so beautiful tonight, is your 'night business' good?... How old are you?..." They said to each other first, and when they saw me coming, the rat eyes quickly turned around and sized me up before asking.

"What? Sir, please speak cleanly. This is a place to drink tea, not..." Seeing that they were talking more and more nonsense, I quickly put on a stern face to stop them from continuing.

"It's okay to ask if your tea business at night is good, why put on such a face! I spent money to drink tea, and I still have to put up with your attitude..." The rat eyes flushed red, and he stood up angrily, as if he disdained drinking my tea.

"Go, go, don't drink it; what celestial being can't be found? With money, you don't have to worry about no one carrying you!" The big guy snatched the words.

"How much money? Here's your change!" He threw two dollars on the table, and with a "clang," one rolled down. Of course, I was the one who gave in, and I immediately picked it up for him. They swarmed behind me and followed me to the counter to get the change.

Not good! When I turned back to collect the cups, the five cups were suddenly gone. I asked the other young ladies, and they all said they didn't take them. Needless to say, it wasn't those troublemakers just now, who else could it be? I understood that I didn't know how to cater to them; but I still don't understand how far my profession requires me to cater to customers.

Continued publication of Special Issue on Women Workers' Lives

Mass Life

Aviation Donation 280

— Little Friend

Bookbinding worker

My sister recently found a job, which is bookbinding work at the XX Bookstore. The salary is six silver dollars a month, without room and board. She understands very well: six dollars a month certainly won't buy enough wine to get drunk, or enough food to get full, or enough to rent a small room, but compared to having no income at all, and facing cold looks from her elderly father all day long, it is much more comfortable. So she gritted her teeth and went to work at the factory.

Alas! Since my sister's husband died and she moved in with my family, her face has been pale, her brows tightly locked, and she has never shown a trace of a smile. She is very casual about what she wears, eats, and drinks. My father, unable to stand it, often scolded her like this: "Burden, debt collector... Money-losing product!"

When she heard this, she didn't say a word, but her brows furrowed even more.

Now she is different. When she gets up in the morning, she combs her hair very smoothly, hides her greasy cloth shirt, and seems to have a happy look on her face, because she hears that after three months, she will be able to live independently.

乂乂乂乂

"Everyone listen up! The company sent out a notice this morning, saying: "The Japanese have seized Rehe! During this time of national crisis, we will implement 'Aviation to Save the Nation.' Everyone must pay an 'Aviation Donation' of two yuan within half a month." A foreman-like figure held up a piece of paper and said to the female workers.

"We don't acknowledge it! We don't acknowledge it! We can't donate that much! We only have eight silver dollars a month in total, how are we supposed to live?" Forty or fifty female workers shouted in a chaotic chorus.

"Whether you acknowledge it or not, this is the boss's order."

"Is there any reason for this?... Mr. Wang!"

"This, this, this is not..."

乂乂乂乂

Half a month has passed, and the female workers' wages have all been paid. Everyone is silent. Only the sound of their whispers can be heard on the road...

"Damn it! Save the nation? Save the nation? Save it into the arms of the foreign devils! Save it into his mother's pocket! Is this how you save the nation?"

My sister returned home, threw the one silver dollar she received on the table, and sighed: "This is half a month's wages!" Looking at her face, it was as pale as it was half a month ago!

Self-Employment Introduction

Please Save a Girl 281

— Ms. Zhu Yongli

Child Laborer

I am a fourteen-year-old girl. I came from the countryside a few months ago and encountered the war in Shanghai. At that time, my family lived in Jiangwan. We fled in the countryside for a few months, and finally fled to Shanghai. My father also had nothing to do, and the whole family was just waiting to starve. It happened that we met a woman from our hometown who worked in the Hengfeng Yarn Factory on Yangshupu Road, and my father asked her to take me in. I learned for a month, learned it, and could handle ninety heads (equivalent to half of an adult worker), but there was no pay, it was said to be savings. I worked for another month, still with no pay. It wasn't until the third month that I received one dollar, but the snack money every day was one hundred wen, which was three thousand wen a month. In terms of the foreign exchange rate at that time, one dollar wasn't even enough. If I did something wrong in the factory, I would be scolded and whipped. I didn't want to go, but at home I would be beaten by my father. Of course, my father couldn't bear to beat his daughter, but he did it for the sake of the family's livelihood! I got up at five in the morning every day and left work at six in the evening. By the time I got home, it was already seven o'clock, because the place I lived was far from the factory. At first, I didn't know the way, and my father had to pick me up and drop me off every day. My mother got up in the middle of the night to cook for me, because the weather was very hot at that time, and the overnight rice often fermented and couldn't be eaten the next day. Therefore, the whole family was very busy for me to work. I worked for four months and still only received one dollar. At this time, my body was getting weaker and weaker, and I couldn't remember many of the books I had read before, so I asked my father not to work anymore. My father had no choice but to say with a bitter face: "Okay, let's not do it!" I stayed at home for a few days and ran to the factory to get my savings. I said to a fat man: "I'm going back to the countryside, please calculate my savings for me." Who knew he sneered and said: "You can't get savings after working for a few months." Alas! I ran home with my head drooping like this. But when I think back to these four months of life, it was simply worse than being a cow or a horse, especially working the night shift. You can't be lazy for a moment, and even going to the toilet has a set time. If you fall asleep in the toilet because you are too tired, and Wen runs over and sees you, he will either beat you or scold you for being a pig. I used to think that the peasants in the countryside were the most miserable, but now when I see the workers in the city, they are a hundred times more miserable than the peasants! I have now left that hell, but the sisters who used to work with me, who are about the same age as me, are still dragging their thin and yellow bodies in and out of that hell every day.

Now, I am unemployed, but I still want to find some better things to do to help my father. I have a high school diploma. I am willing to do any kind of work as a female trainee in companies, businesses, and other institutions. As for the salary, it doesn't matter how much or how little; I think the gentlemen who read this magazine will not bully this poor girl. Please forward the correspondence address through this magazine.
